| campaignbox       = {{October 7 attacks}} {{Campaignbox Gaza war}}
}}

The '''October 7 attacks''' were a series of coordinated armed incursions from the [[Gaza Strip]] into the [[Gaza envelope]] of [[Southern District (Israel)|southern Israel]], carried out by [[Hamas]] and several other Palestinian militant groups in 2023, during the Jewish holiday of [[Simchat Torah]]. The attacks, which began the ongoing [[Gaza war]], were the first large-scale invasion of [[Israel|Israeli territory]] since the [[1948 Arab–Israeli War]]. In response, Israel launched [[Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|a large-scale military operation in Gaza]].

The attacks began with a [[List of Palestinian rocket attacks on Israel in 2023|barrage of at least 4,300 rockets]] launched into Israel<ref name=":18">{{Cite news |date=August 31, 2024 |title=Probe reveals 6,000 Gazans infiltrated Israel during October 7 massacre – report |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-817176 |access-date=September 1, 2024 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |language=en |archive-date=August 31, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240831221239/https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-817176 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=":19">{{Cite news |title=Report: New IDF assessment shows some 6,000 Gazans invaded Israel on Oct. 7 |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/report-new-idf-assessment-shows-some-6000-gazans-invaded-israel-on-oct-7/ |access-date=September 1, 2024 |archive-date=September 20, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240920121730/https://www.timesofisrael.com/report-new-idf-assessment-shows-some-6000-gazans-invaded-israel-on-oct-7/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=":16" /> and vehicle-transported and [[powered paraglider]] incursions into Israel.<ref name="Kubovich Day 1">{{cite news |last1=Kubovich |first1=Yaniv |title=The First Hours of the Israel-Hamas War: What Actually Took Place? According to an [[Israel Defense Forces]] (IDF) report that revised the estimate on the number of attackers, 6,000 Gazans breached the border in 119 locations into Israel, including 3,800 from the elite [[Nukhba forces]] and 2,200 civilians and other militants.<ref name=":15">{{Cite news |title=Doubling previous numbers, report says 6,000 Gazans – including 3,800 trained Hamas terrorists – broke into Israel on Oct. 7 |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/doubling-previous-numbers-report-says-6000-gazans-including-3800-trained-hamas-terrorists-broke-into-israel-on-oct-7/ |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |access-date=August 31, 2024 |archive-date=September 1, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240901041345/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/doubling-previous-numbers-report-says-6000-gazans-including-3800-trained-hamas-terrorists-broke-into-israel-on-oct-7/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=":18" /><ref name=":19" /> Additionally, the IDF report estimated 1,000 Gazans fired rockets from the Gaza Strip, bringing the total number of participants on Hamas's side to 7,000.<ref name=":15" /><ref name=":18" /><ref name=":19" />

== Background ==
{{further|Background to the Gaza war|Israeli–Palestinian conflict}}
[[File:OCHA OpT September 2023 map of the Gaza Strip.pdf|thumb|429x429px|The [[Gaza Strip]] under [[Blockade of the Gaza Strip|Israeli blockade]], with Israeli/Egyptian-controlled borders and limited fishing zone in September 2023.]]

Israel has occupied the [[Palestinian territories]], including the Gaza Strip, since the [[Six-Day War]] in 1967.<ref>{{cite news |title=Original sin: on the attack on Israel and the occupation of Palestine |work=[[The Hindu]] |url=https://www.thehindu.com/opinion/editorial/original-sin-on-the-attack-on-israel-and-the-occupation-of-palestine/article67400015.ece |access-date=October 10, 2023 |archive-date=October 10, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231010081312/https://www.thehindu.com/opinion/editorial/original-sin-on-the-attack-on-israel-and-the-occupation-of-palestine/article67400015.ece |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=Arab Perspectives on the Middle East Crisis |url=https://carnegieendowment.org/posts/2023/10/arab-perspectives-on-the-middle-east-crisis?lang=en |publisher=[[Carnegie Endowment for International Peace]] |access-date=November 7, 2023 |archive-date=November 16, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231116150803/https://carnegieendowment.org/2023/10/13/arab-perspectives-on-middle-east-crisis-pub-90774 |url-status=live}}</ref> In 2005, [[Israeli disengagement from the Gaza Strip|Israel disengaged]] from the Gaza Strip by dismantling all 21 [[Israeli settlement]]s there.<ref name="britannica">{{Cite web |title=Israel's disengagement from Gaza (2005) {{!}} Withdrawal, Map, & Hamas {{!}} Britannica |url=https://www.britannica.com/event/Israels-disengagement-from-Gaza |access-date=2024-05-12 |website=britannica.com |language=en}}</ref> Nonetheless, the Gaza Strip has continued to be regarded by the [[United Nations]], many other international humanitarian and legal organizations, and most academic commentators as being under [[Israeli-occupied territories|Israeli occupation]] due to [[Blockade of the Gaza Strip|Israel's active control over the territory's external affairs]], as affirmed by the [[ICJ case on Israel's occupation of the Palestinian territories|2024 International Court of Justice advisory opinion]].<ref name="occ">{{cite book |last=Sanger |first=Andrew |title=Yearbook of International Humanitarian Law – 2010 |date=2011 |publisher=Springer Science & Business Media |isbn=978-90-6704-811-8 |editor1=M.N. Schmitt |volume=13 |page=429 |chapter=The Contemporary Law of Blockade and the Gaza Freedom Flotilla |doi=10.1007/978-90-6704-811-8_14 |quote=Israel claims it no longer occupies the Gaza Strip, maintaining that it is neither a State nor a territory occupied or controlled by Israel, but rather it has 'sui generis' status. Pursuant to the Disengagement Plan, Israel dismantled all military institutions and settlements in Gaza and there is no longer a permanent Israeli military or civilian presence in the territory. However, the Plan also provided that Israel will guard and monitor the external land perimeter of the Gaza Strip, will continue to maintain exclusive authority in Gaza air space, and will continue to exercise security activity in the sea off the coast of the Gaza Strip as well as maintaining an Israeli military presence on the Egyptian-Gaza border, and reserving the right to reenter Gaza at will. Israel continues to control six of Gaza's seven land crossings, its maritime borders and airspace and the movement of goods and persons in and out of the territory. Egypt controls one of Gaza's land crossings. Gaza is also dependent on Israel for water, electricity, telecommunications and other utilities, currency, issuing IDs, and permits to enter and leave the territory. Israel also has sole control of the Palestinian Population Registry through which the Israeli Army regulates who is classified as a Palestinian and who is a Gazan or West Banker. Since 2000 aside from a limited number of exceptions Israel has refused to add people to the Palestinian Population Registry. It is this direct external control over Gaza and indirect control over life within Gaza that has led the United Nations, the UN General Assembly, the UN Fact Finding Mission to Gaza, International human rights organisations, US Government websites, the UK Foreign and Commonwealth Office and a significant number of legal commentators, to reject the argument that Gaza is no longer occupied. |editor2=Louise Arimatsu |editor3=Tim McCormack |chapter-url=https://books.google.com/books?id=hYiIWVlpFzEC&pg=PA429}}<br />* {{cite book |last=Scobbie |first=Iain |author-link=Iain Scobbie |url=https://books.google.com/books?id=GM90Xp03uuEC&pg=PA295 |title=International Law and the Classification of Conflicts |date=2012 |publisher=Oxford University Press |isbn=978-0-19-965775-9 |editor=Elizabeth Wilmshurst |page=295 |quote=Even after the accession to power of Hamas, Israel's claim that it no longer occupies Gaza has not been accepted by UN bodies, most States, nor the majority of academic commentators because of its exclusive control of its border with Gaza and crossing points including the effective control it exerted over the Rafah crossing until at least May 2011, its control of Gaza's maritime zones and airspace which constitute what Aronson terms the 'security envelope' around Gaza, as well as its ability to intervene forcibly at will in Gaza.}}<br />* {{cite book |last=Gawerc |first=Michelle |url=https://books.google.com/books?id=Hka8FZ4UdWUC&pg=PA44 |title=Prefiguring Peace: Israeli-Palestinian Peacebuilding Partnerships |date=2012 |publisher=Lexington Books |isbn=9780739166109 |page=44 |quote=While Israel withdrew from the immediate territory, it remained in control of all access to and from Gaza through the border crossings, as well as through the coastline and the airspace. In addition, Gaza was dependent upon Israel for water, electricity sewage communication networks and for its trade (Gisha 2007. Dowty 2008). In other words, while Israel maintained that its occupation of Gaza ended with its unilateral disengagement Palestinians – as well as many human rights organizations and international bodies – argued that Gaza was by all intents and purposes still occupied.}}</ref>

The Islamic Resistance Movement ([[Hamas]]), is a [[Palestinian nationalist]]<ref name="natdem" >Theocratic extremist Islamists, affiliates and sympathizers of [[ISIS]] and [[Al Qaeda]], have condemned Hamas for their nationalism and their participation in [[Islam and democracy|electoral politics]]: {{cite news |title=Why Differences between Globalist and Nationalist Armed Islamist Groups Matter |work=MES Insights |volume=14 |number=6 |url=https://www.usmcu.edu/Outreach/Marine-Corps-University-Press/MES-Publications/MES-Insights/Excommunicating-Hamas/ |access-date=August 21, 2024 |date=December 2023 |archive-date=August 21, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240821194747/https://www.usmcu.edu/Outreach/Marine-Corps-University-Press/MES-Publications/MES-Insights/Excommunicating-Hamas/ |url-status=live}}</ref> [[Islamist]] movement. They formed in 1987, and are the largest Islamist movement in the Palestinian territories.<ref name="auto12">{{Cite book |last=Kushner |first=Harvey W. |title=Encyclopedia of terrorism |date=2003 |publisher=[[SAGE Publications]] |isbn=978-0-7619-2408-1 |location=Thousand Oaks (Calif.) London |pages=xxiv}}</ref> They maintain an uncompromising stance on the "complete liberation of Palestine", often using [[Palestinian political violence|political violence]] to achieve their goals.<ref name="auto12" /> Recent statements suggest a shift in focus toward ending the [[Israeli occupation of Palestinian territories]] and establishing a Palestinian state based on the [[1967 borders]]. Hamas has been responsible for numerous suicide bombings<ref>{{Cite journal |last1=Dolnik |first1=A. |last2=Bhattacharjee |first2=A. |date=2002 |title=Hamas: Suicide Bombings, Rockets, or WMD? |url=http://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1080/714005624 |url-status=live |journal=Terrorism and Political Violence |language= |volume=14 |issue=3 |pages=109–128 |doi=10.1080/714005624 |issn=0954-6553 |s2cid=143776419 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240206101232/https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1080/714005624 |archive-date=February 6, 2024 |access-date=February 1, 2024 |quote=Hamas' initial involvement in the violent exchange dates to 1989, when the group conducted a stabbing campaign against individual Israelis. ... when Hamas launched a series of suicide bombings accompanied by several kidnappings of Israeli soldiers. Suicide operations remain the most dominant Hamas tactic to date, along with occasional shooting, grenade and time bomb attacks.|url-access=subscription }}</ref><ref>{{Cite journal |last=Litvak |first=Meir |date=July 15, 2010 |title="Martyrdom is Life": Jihad and Martyrdom in the Ideology of Hamas |url=https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/full/10.1080/1057610X.2010.494170 |url-status=live |journal=Studies in Conflict & Terrorism |volume=33 |issue=8 |pages=716–734 |doi=10.1080/1057610X.2010.494170 |issn=1057-610X |s2cid=144566931 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231212103657/https://www.tandfonline.com/doi/full/10.1080/1057610X.2010.494170 |archive-date=December 12, 2023 |access-date=February 1, 2024 |quote=In the course of time, Hamas has become the most effective Palestinian organization fighting Israel, carrying out a series of suicide attacks, against mostly civilian Israeli targets, in the years 1994–1996 and 2001–2007, which caused the death of over 1,000 Israeli civilians.|url-access=subscription }}</ref> and rocket attacks targeting Israeli civilians.<ref>{{Cite web |date=August 12, 2021 |title=Rights group says Hamas rockets at Israel a clear war crime |url=https://apnews.com/article/middle-east-business-israel-race-and-ethnicity-racial-injustice-1032a5117375ba8c0cdffbdd62ce02ad |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231204154541/https://apnews.com/article/middle-east-business-israel-race-and-ethnicity-racial-injustice-1032a5117375ba8c0cdffbdd62ce02ad |archive-date=December 4, 2023 |access-date=December 7, 2023 |website=AP News}}</ref> Australia, Canada, the EU, Japan, New Zealand, and the UK have designated Hamas a "terrorist organisation". In 2010 it attempted to derail the peace talks between Israel and the PA. In 2017, it adopted a [[2017 Hamas charter|new charter]], removing [[antisemitic]] language and shifting focus from Jews to Zionists.<ref>

=== Warnings ===
Before the attack, Saudi Arabia warned Israel of an "explosion" as a result of the continued occupation,<ref name="edwardwong">{{Cite news |last1=Wong |first1=Edward |last2=Nereim |first2=Vivian |date=October 7, 2023 |title=The war could upend Biden's diplomacy on Saudi-Israel normalization. |work=[[The New York Times]] |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/07/world/middleeast/saudi-israel-gaza-war.html |access-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008012102/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/07/world/middleeast/saudi-israel-gaza-war.html |url-status=live |url-access=limited}}</ref> and Egypt had warned of a catastrophe.<ref>{{cite news |date= October 12, 2023|title= Egypt warned Israel days before Hamas struck, US committee chairman says
|url= https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67082047|work= BBC |access-date=July 3, 2025}}</ref>

=== Events leading to the attack ===
{{see also|Timeline of the Israeli–Palestinian conflict in 2023}}

Throughout 2023, increased settler attacks displaced hundreds of Palestinians.<ref name="apn1">{{Cite news |last1=Goldberg |first1=Tia |last2=Shurafa |first2=Wafaa |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Israel declares war, goes after Hamas fighters and bombards Gaza |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-ca7903976387cfc1e1011ce9ea805a71 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008051308/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-ca7903976387cfc1e1011ce9ea805a71 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |access-date=October 7, 2023 |work=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref> <!--Clashes near Nablus on 5 and 6 October, too last-minute to be inciting, but relevant to context of ongoing tensions. Reported in multiple very reliable sources, but not much detail. Noting here for someone else to follow up if I forget. --> In April, [[2023 Al-Aqsa clashes|clashes occurred around the Al-Aqsa Mosque]], a contested holy site in Jerusalem. In May, [[May 2023 Gaza–Israel clashes|clashes occurred]] between Israel and the [[Palestinian Islamic Jihad]] group.<ref name="apn1"/>

Tensions between Israel and Hamas rose in September 2023, and ''[[The Washington Post]]'' wrote that the two were "on the brink of war".<ref name=wapo>{{cite news |title=What's behind the violence in Israel and Gaza? were killed at the border.{{efn|''[[The Washington Post]]'' said the Palestinians were trying to explode the device,<ref name="wapo" /> while Al-Jazeera said that a Palestinian Explosives Engineering ===Operational planning===
For two years, Hamas used [[Landline|hardwired phone lines]] within Gaza's tunnel network, nicknamed the "[[Gaza metro]]", to covertly communicate, evade Israeli intelligence, and plan Operation Al-Aqsa Flood.<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Brown |first1=Pamela |last2=Cohen |first2=Zachary |date=October 24, 2023 |title=Hamas operatives used phone lines installed in tunnels under Gaza to plan Israel attack over 2 years, sources familiar with intelligence say |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/24/politics/intelligence-hamas-israel-attack-tunnels-phone-lines/index.html |access-date=December 11, 2024 |work=[[CNN]] |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Beaumont |first=Peter |date=October 28, 2023 |title='A spider's web of tunnels': inside Gaza's underground network being targeted by Israel |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/28/a-spiders-web-of-tunnels-inside-gazas-underground-network-being-targeted-by-israel |access-date=December 11, 2024 |work=[[The Observer]] |language=en-GB |issn=0029-7712}}</ref>

In the months preceding the attack, Hamas publicly released videos of its militants preparing to attack Israel. A video released in December 2022 showed Hamas training to take hostages, while another video showed Hamas practicing [[paragliding]].<ref>{{Cite news |title=Hamas militants trained for its deadly attack in plain sight and less than a mile from Israel's heavily fortified border |first1=Paul P. |last1=Murphy |first2=Tara |last2=John |first3=Brent |last3=Swails |first4=Oren |last4=Liebermann |date=October 13, 2023|url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/12/middleeast/hamas-training-site-gaza-israel-intl/index.html |access-date=October 13, 2023 |work=[[CNN]] |archive-date=October 13, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231013024259/https://www.cnn.com/2023/10/12/middleeast/hamas-training-site-gaza-israel-intl/index.html |url-status=live}}</ref> On September 12, Hamas posted a video of its fighters training to blast through the border.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/hamas-practised-in-plain-sight-posting-video-of-mock-attack-weeks-before-border-breach/ |title=Hamas practised in plain sight, posting video of mock attack weeks before border breach |date=October 12, 2023 |work=[[CTV News]] |access-date=November 17, 2023 |archive-date=November 17, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231117064305/https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/hamas-practised-in-plain-sight-posting-video-of-mock-attack-weeks-before-border-breach-1.6599556 |url-status=live}}</ref> After the attack, the IDF said that Hamas had extensively studied the military bases and communities near the border.<ref name=":0">{{cite news |last=Schecter |first=Anna |date=October 14, 2023 |title='Top secret' Hamas documents show that terrorists intentionally targeted elementary schools and a youth center |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/news/investigations/top-secret-hamas-documents-show-terrorists-intentionally-targeted-elem-rcna120310 |access-date=October 14, 2023 |work=[[NBC News]] |archive-date=October 14, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231014000228/https://www.nbcnews.com/news/investigations/top-secret-hamas-documents-show-terrorists-intentionally-targeted-elem-rcna120310 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Morris |first1=Loveday |last2=Hendrix |first2=Steve |title=Documents found on fighters reveal Hamas capabilities, bloody plans |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/21/hamas-documents-plans-israel-attack/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231023110256/https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/21/hamas-documents-plans-israel-attack/ |archive-date=October 23, 2023 |access-date=October 30, 2023 |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]]}}</ref>

''[[The Wall Street Journal]]'' has accused Iran of being behind the attack.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Said |first1=Summer |last2=Faucon |first2=Benoit |last3=Stephen |first3=Kalin |date=October 8, 2023 |title=Iran Helped Plot Attack on Israel Over Several Weeks |url=https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/iran-israel-hamas-strike-planning-bbe07b25 |work=[[The Wall Street Journal]] |access-date=December 10, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231008204919/https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/iran-israel-hamas-strike-planning-bbe07b25 |url-status=live |url-access=subscription}}</ref> U.S. officials<ref name="Training">{{cite news |title=500 Hamas, PIJ terrorists trained for October 7 attack in Iran last month – report |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/500-hamas-pij-terrorists-trained-for-october-7-attack-in-iran-last-month-report/ |access-date=October 27, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=October 25, 2023 |archive-date=October 26, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026232038/https://www.timesofisrael.com/500-hamas-pij-terrorists-trained-for-october-7-attack-in-iran-last-month-report/ |url-status=live}}</ref> and Iran have denied this.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/irans-un-mission-says-tehran-not-involved-hamas-attacks-2023-10-09/ |title=Iran's UN mission says Tehran not involved in Hamas attacks |date=October 9, 2023 |newspaper=[[Reuters]] |access-date=November 17, 2023 |archive-date=October 9, 2023|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009033748/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/irans-un-mission-says-tehran-not-involved-hamas-attacks-2023-10-09/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

According to a [[The New York Times|New York Times]] investigation, a memo dated August 24, 2022, and apparently written by [[Yahya Sinwar]] described a Hamas attack on Israel similar to October 7 attacks. It called for bulldozers to breach the Gaza-Israel fence and for multiple assault waves. It urged "Stomp on the heads of soldiers" and listed "opening fire on soldiers at point-blank range, slaughtering some of them with knives, blowing up tanks". It ordered entry into residential areas to set them on fire "with gasoline or diesel from a tanker", preparing "two or three operations" in which "an entire neighborhood, kibbutz, or something similar will be burned". It directed unit commanders to film and broadcast the acts to mobilize Palestinians in the West Bank, Arabs in Israel, and "our nation" to "join the revolution".<ref name=":1">{{Cite news |date=October 11, 2025 |title=A Memo in a Bunker, Intercepted Communications and Hamas's Oct. 7 Plans |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2025/10/11/world/middleeast/israel-hamas-plans.html |access-date=October 12, 2025 |language=en}}</ref>

The IDF reportedly seized over 10,000 weapons following the attack. The arsenal included RPGs, mines, sniper rifles, drones, [[thermobaric]] rockets, and other advanced weapons. According to Israeli sources, documents and maps seized from Hamas militants indicated that Hamas intended a coordinated, month-long operation to invade and occupy Israeli towns, cities, and kibbutzim, including attacking [[Ashkelon]] by sea and reaching [[Kiryat Gat]], 20 miles (32&nbsp;km) into Israel. The scale of weapons, supplies, and plans indicated, according to Israel, that Hamas intended to inflict mass casualties on Israeli civilians and military forces over an extended period.<ref>{{cite news |last=Zitun |first=Yoav |title=Captured weapons shed light on stunning extent of Hamas's battle blueprint |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/ry4wgk9116 |work=[[Ynetnews]] |date=October 16, 2023 |access-date=November 6, 2023 |archive-date=November 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107121128/https://www.ynetnews.com/article/ry4wgk9116 |url-status=live}}</ref> Western and Middle Eastern security officials gathered evidence suggesting that Hamas intended to invade as far as the West Bank, had the initial attack been more successful.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/gaza-news/article-772934 |title=Hamas planned to push October 7 massacre to the West Bank border – report |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |date=November 12, 2023 |access-date=November 14, 2023 |archive-date=November 14, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231114055918/https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/gaza-news/article-772934 |url-status=live}}</ref>

===Israeli intelligence failure===
According to ''[[The New York Times]]'', Israeli officials had obtained detailed attack plans more than a year before the attack. The document described operational plans and targets, including the size and location of Israeli forces, and raised questions in Israel about how Hamas learned these details. The document provided a plan that included a large-scale rocket assault before an invasion, drones to knock out the surveillance cameras and automated guns that Israel has stationed along the border, and gunmen invading Israel, including with paragliders. ''[[The Times]]'' reported, "Hamas followed the blueprint with shocking precision." According to ''The Times'', the document was widely circulated among Israeli military and intelligence leadership, who largely dismissed the plan as beyond Hamas's capabilities, though it was unclear whether the political leadership was informed. In July 2023, a member of the [[Unit 8200|Israeli signals intelligence unit]] alerted her superiors that Hamas was conducting preparations for the assault, saying, "I utterly refute that the scenario is imaginary". An Israeli colonel ignored her concerns.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bergman |first1=Ronen |last2=Goldman |first2=Adam |title=Israel Knew Hamas's Attack Plan Over a Year Ago |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=December 1, 2023 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/30/world/middleeast/israel-hamas-attack-intelligence.html?campaign_id=307&emc=edit_igwb_20231201&instance_id=109019&nl=israel-hamas-war-briefing&regi_id=64680187&segment_id=151409&te=1&user_id=1e9c9142246ac5796beabc2f49486341 |access-date=December 1, 2023 |archive-date=December 6, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231206180618/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/30/world/middleeast/israel-hamas-attack-intelligence.html?campaign_id=307&emc=edit_igwb_20231201&instance_id=109019&nl=israel-hamas-war-briefing&regi_id=64680187&segment_id=151409&te=1&user_id=1e9c9142246ac5796beabc2f49486341 |url-status=live}}</ref>

The official investigation by Israel's domestic intelligence agency, [[Shin Bet]], found that the agency failed to provide the warning that could have prevented the massacre. The head of Shin Bet convened a situation assessment in the early hours of October 7 to discuss the intelligence received from Gaza; in the end, only a low-level warning was issued, and a small team specialising in thwarting limited attacks was sent to the south. According to the report the counterintelligence service of Hamas had been highly effective in preventing the gathering of intelligence in Gaza.<ref name=shabak>{{cite news |title=Probing October 7, Shin Bet Points Fingers at Netanyahu, Fueling Tensions With PM |access-date=March 11, 2025 |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=March 5, 2025 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-03-05/ty-article/.premium/shin-bet-oct-7-probe-finds-internal-failures-points-finger-at-prime-minister/00000195-62f1-db7b-afdd-f2fdc8cb0000 |first=Amos |last=Harel |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250305041235/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-03-05/ty-article/.premium/shin-bet-oct-7-probe-finds-internal-failures-points-finger-at-prime-minister/00000195-62f1-db7b-afdd-f2fdc8cb0000 |archive-date=March 5, 2025}}</ref>

According to the findings of the investigation, Shin Bet warned the Prime Minister that Hamas was not deterred and objected to the prevailing divide-and-rule policy of the Israeli government.<ref name=shabak/>

According to ''[[Haaretz]]'', [[Shin Bet]] and IDF military commanders discussed a possible threat to the Nova music festival near kibbutz [[Re'im]] just hours before the attack, but the festival's organizers were not warned.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Kubovich |first1=Yaniv |title=Despite Israeli Intelligence Warnings About a Hamas Attack, the Army Didn't Evacuate the Nova Festival |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-05/ty-article/.premium/despite-intel-warnings-about-a-hamas-attack-the-army-didnt-evacuate-the-nova-festival/0000018c-3993-dc03-a9ec-3dfb2cda0000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=December 5, 2023 |access-date=December 10, 2023 |archive-date=December 5, 2023 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231205200823/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-05/ty-article/.premium/despite-intel-warnings-about-a-hamas-attack-the-army-didnt-evacuate-the-nova-festival/0000018c-3993-dc03-a9ec-3dfb2cda0000 |url-status=live |url-access=subscription}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last=Grylls |first=George |date=December 6, 2023 |title=Nova festival: Israel 'withheld warnings' about Hamas massacre |url=https://www.thetimes.com/world/middle-east/article/israel-nova-music-festival-shin-bet-hamas-massacre-wv7qs3cww |work=[[The Times]] |location=London |access-date=September 14, 2025 |archive-date=August 26, 2025 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250826010149/https://www.thetimes.com/world/middle-east/article/israel-nova-music-festival-shin-bet-hamas-massacre-wv7qs3cww |url-status=live}}</ref>

As revealed by a [[BBC]] investigation, surveillance reports suggested that Hamas was planning a significant operation against Israel, but senior IDF officers repeatedly ignored the warnings.<ref name="Cuddy">{{cite news |last=Cuddy |first=Alice |date=January 15, 2024 |title=They were Israel's 'eyes on the border' – but their Hamas warnings went unheard |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-67958260 |work=[[BBC News]] |access-date=January 15, 2024 |archive-date=January 15, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240115002359/https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-67958260 |url-status=live}}</ref>

A ''Haaretz'' investigation found that incompetence in the IDF's higher ranks, including refusal to acknowledge Hamas's preparations for the attacks, was a major contributor to the severity of the October attacks. The IDF had reduced funding and manpower dedicated to observing Hamas, focusing primarily on rocket sites and ignoring Hamas training and troop movements, and the activities of the Hamas military leadership. Exercises in which Hamas attacks were simulated found the Gaza division's response lacking. [[Cultural conformity]] was fostered among officers and dissent discouraged. Senior officers often silenced subordinates to maintain their positions, contributing to a [[Toxic workplace|toxic atmosphere]] in which lower-ranking officers were apprehensive about questioning the decisions of their superiors - and tended to refrain from doing so.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Kubovich |first1=Yaniv |title=Disdain, denial, neglect: The deep roots of Israel's devastating intelligence failure on Hamas and October 7 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-05-09/ty-article/.premium/disdain-denial-neglect-the-roots-of-israels-intelligence-failure-on-hamas-and-oct-7/0000018f-5811-d348-a7bf-feb907a80000 |access-date=May 11, 2024 |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=May 9, 2024 |url-access=subscription |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250803192603/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-05-09/ty-article/.premium/disdain-denial-neglect-the-roots-of-israels-intelligence-failure-on-hamas-and-oct-7/0000018f-5811-d348-a7bf-feb907a80000 |archive-date=August 3, 2025}}</ref>

==Attacks==
{{main list|List of military engagements during the Gaza war
}}

At around 6:30&nbsp;a.m. [[Israel Summer Time]] (UTC+3) on Saturday, October 7, 2023, Hamas announced the start of Operation Al-Aqsa Flood.<ref name="aj1">{{Cite news |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/sirens-warn-of-rockets-launched-towards-israel-from-gaza-news-reports |title=Israel retaliation kills 230 Palestinians after Hamas operation |date=October 7, 2023 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |access-date=October 18, 2023 |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007053106/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/sirens-warn-of-rockets-launched-towards-israel-from-gaza-news-reports |url-status=live}}</ref> [[Al-Qassam Brigades]] commander [[Mohammed Deif]] gave a speech mentioning Israel's [[Blockade of the Gaza Strip|16-year blockade of Gaza]], Israeli incursions in West Bank cities, violence at Al-Aqsa mosque, [[Israeli settler violence]] with the army's support, the confiscation of property and demolition of homes, arbitrarily detaining Palestinians for years until "they wither from cancer and disease", Israel's neglect for international law, American-Western support, and international silence. He then described the operation, that they had drawn the line, and that it was to end "the last occupation on Earth".<ref>{{cite news |title=Hamas leader Haniyeh: Battle 'will spread to West Bank, Jerusalem' |date=October 8, 2023 |url=https://www.arabnews.com/node/2387276/middle-east |agency=[[Associated Press]] and [[Reuters]] |quote="The leader of Hamas' military wing, Mohammed Deif, said Saturday's assault was in response to the 16-year blockade of Gaza, Israeli raids inside West Bank cities over the past year, violence at Al-Aqsa and increasing attacks by settlers on Palestinians, and growth of settlements." |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231018143356/https://www.arabnews.com/node/2387276/middle-east |archive-date=October 18, 2023}}</ref><ref name="aj1"/> Shortly thereafter,  [[Ismail Haniyeh]] made a similar announcement in a televised address.<ref>{{cite news |title=Hundreds dead as war erupts after surprise Hamas attack catches Israel off guard |date=October 7, 2023 |url=https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/gaza-israel-rockets-attack-hamas-1.6990209 |agency=[[Associated Press]] |work=[[Canadian Broadcasting Corporation|CBC]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240110155357/https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/gaza-israel-rockets-attack-hamas-1.6990209 |archive-date=January 10, 2024}}</ref>

=== Participating and supporting organizations ===

In addition to Hamas, several Palestinian militant groups voiced support for the operation and participated in it to some extent. The [[National Resistance Brigades]], the armed wing of the [[Maoism|Maoist]] [[Democratic Front for the Liberation of Palestine]] (DFLP), confirmed their participation in the operation through their military spokesman [[Abu Khaled (DFLP)|Abu Khaled]],<ref>{{Cite web |script-title=ar:"أبو خالد" الناطق العسكري لكتائب المقاومة الوطنية (قوات الشهيد عمر القاسم) الجناح العسكري للجبهة الديمقراطية لتحرير فلسطين |trans-title=[Statement from] "Abu Khalid", the military spokesperson for the National Resistance Brigades (the military wing of the Democratic Front for the Liberation of Palestine). |url=https://alhourriah.org/article/125236 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008113130/https://alhourriah.org/article/125236 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |access-date=October 8, 2023 |publisher=[[Al-Hurriya (newspaper)|Al-Hurriya]] |language=ar}}</ref> saying it had lost three fighters in combat with the IDF.<ref name="DFLP"/> The [[PFLP]] (a Palestinian Marxist–Leninist / secular nationalist political party)<ref name="pflp"/> and the [[Lions' Den (militant group)|Lions' Den]] group (a nonpartisan militant group based in the [[West Bank]]) voiced support for the operation and declared maximum alertness and general mobilization among their troops. Nine individuals employed by [[UNRWA]] were accused by Israel of participation, and after a months-long internal investigation, were fired for possible involvement.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/08/05/unrwa-october-7-israel-hamas-gaza/ |title=U.N. fires Gaza staff, citing possible involvement in attack on Israel |first=Karen |last=DeYoung |date=August 5, 2024 |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=August 10, 2024 |archive-date=August 7, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240807091206/https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2024/08/05/unrwa-october-7-israel-hamas-gaza/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

=== Incursions into southern Israel ===

[[File:Hamas terrorists fire into moving civilian car near Sderot police station during October 7 attacks.webm|thumb|Hamas militants fire into a moving civilian car in [[Sderot]].]]
[[File:Hamas members attacking civilians in Kibbutz Mefalsim, Israel (October 2023).webm|thumb|Militants killing Israelis in kibbutz [[Mefalsim]].]]

Simultaneously, around 6,000 Palestinian militants and civilians infiltrated Israel from Gaza breaching the border in 119 places.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Dov |first1=Yehuda |title=Huge Arsenal Of Weapons Indicate: Hamas Planned To Invade Ashkelon, Kiryat Gat |url=https://vinnews.com/2023/10/16/huge-arsenal-of-weapons-indicate-hamas-planned-to-invade-ashkelon-kiryat-gat/ |access-date=October 16, 2023 |work=VINnews |archive-date=October 17, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231017020444/https://vinnews.com/2023/10/16/huge-arsenal-of-weapons-indicate-hamas-planned-to-invade-ashkelon-kiryat-gat/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=":18" /><ref name=":19" /> The infiltration was executed using trucks, [[pickup truck]]s, motorcycles, bulldozers, speedboats, and [[Powered paragliding|powered paraglider]]s.<ref name="ap1">{{Cite news |last1=Federman |first1=Josef |last2=Adwan |first2=Issam |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Hamas militant group has started a war that 'Israel will win,' defense minister says |work=[[Associated Press]] |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-11fb98655c256d54ecb5329284fc37d2 |url-status=live |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007073124/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-11fb98655c256d54ecb5329284fc37d2 |archive-date=October 7, 2023}}</ref><ref name="aj1" /><ref name="nyt7oct">{{Cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Gaza and Israel in 'War Mode' After Militants Launch Surprise Assaults |work=[[The New York Times]] |url=https://www.nytimes.com/live/2023/10/07/world/israel-gaza-attack |url-status=live |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007075901/https://www.nytimes.com/live/2023/10/07/world/israel-gaza-attack |archive-date=October 7, 2023}}</ref>

In a raid on the Sderot police station, 30 Israeli policemen and civilians were killed.<ref name="Margulies">{{cite news |last=Margulies |first=Joanie |date=October 8, 2023 |title=IDF regains control over Sderot police station |newspaper=Jerusalem Post |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/defense-news/article-763198 |access-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007170438/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/gunmen-homes-captives-abducted-gaza-leave-israelis-shock-2023-10-07/ |url-status=live}}</ref>
Early in the attack the computer systems were destroyed,  disabling communication and delaying the response to the attacks.<ref name="Dr. Levi West - tactics to strategy/">{{cite news |last1=Darnley-Stuart |first1=Adam |last2=West |first2=Levi |title=MWI Podcast: Understanding Hamas—from Tactics to Strategy |url=https://mwi.westpoint.edu/mwi-podcast-understanding-hamas-from-tactics-to-strategy/ |access-date=January 5, 2024 |publisher=Modern War Institute at West Point |date=November 14, 2023 |archive-date=January 6, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240106001052/https://mwi.westpoint.edu/mwi-podcast-understanding-hamas-from-tactics-to-strategy/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="iaudio Dr. Levi West - Modern War Institute">{{cite news |last1=Darnley-Stuart |first1=Adam |last2=West |first2=Levi |title=Modern War Institute: Understanding Hamas: From Tactics to Strategy on Apple Podcasts |url=https://podcasts.apple.com/au/podcast/understanding-hamas-from-tactics-to-strategy/id1079958510?i=1000634767004 |access-date=January 5, 2024 |publisher=Modern War Institute at West Point |via=Apple Podcasts |archive-date=January 6, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240106001050/https://podcasts.apple.com/au/podcast/understanding-hamas-from-tactics-to-strategy/id1079958510?i=1000634767004 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="Levi West - Irregular Warfare Podcast">{{cite news |last1=West |first1=Levi |last2=Darnley-Stuart |first2=Adam |title=Irregular Warfare Podcast: Taking the Long View on Hamas on Apple Podcasts |url=https://podcasts.apple.com/us/podcast/taking-the-long-view-on-hamas/id1514636385?i=1000634764141 |access-date=January 6, 2024 |work=Irregular Warfare Podcast |publisher=Modern War Institute at West Point |via=iTunes |archive-date=January 6, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240106015516/https://podcasts.apple.com/us/podcast/taking-the-long-view-on-hamas/id1514636385?i=1000634764141 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Images and videos on social media showed heavily armed and masked militants dressed in black fatigues riding pickup trucks<ref name="bbc1" /><ref name="cnn1" /> and opening fire in Sderot, killing dozens of Israeli civilians and soldiers and setting homes on fire.<ref name="f24-2">{{cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=In pictures: Scenes of war and chaos after Hamas launch surprise attack on Israel |work=[[France 24]] |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20231007-in-pictures-hamas-israel-palestine-gaza-attack-netanyahu |url-status=live |access-date=October 7, 2023 Other videos appeared to show Israelis taken prisoner, a burning Israeli tank,<ref name="AP">{{Cite news |last1=Federman |first1=Josef |last2=Adwan |first2=Issam |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Hamas militant group launches unprecedented operation against Israel with rockets and infiltration 2023 |access-date=October 10, 2023 |work=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref><ref name="guardian7oct" /> and militants driving Israeli military vehicles.<ref name="bbc1" /> Israeli first responders  recovered documents from militants' bodies with instructions to attack civilians, including elementary schools and a youth center, to "kill as many people as possible", and to take hostages for use in future negotiations.<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Robinson |first1=Adele |last2=Taylor |first2=Jack |last3=Elms |first3=Victoria |date=October 13, 2023 |title='Top secret' documents seen by Sky News suggest Hamas The UN's [[Pramila Patten]] and [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory|Commission of Inquiry]] concluded in their reports that the authenticity of these alleged instruction documents, claimed to have been retrieved from Hamas militants, could not be substantiated.<ref name=":13"/><ref name="OHCHR3">{{cite report Some of the militants wore [[body camera]]s to record the acts, presumably for propaganda purposes.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tolan |first1=Casey |last2=Ash |first2=Audrey |last3=Chapman |first3=Isabelle during the attack, published by The New York Times, one commander is heard saying: "Document the scenes of horror, now, and broadcast them on TV channels to the whole world", and "Slaughter them. End the children of Israel".<ref name=":1" />

The morning of the attack, an Israeli military spokesman said that the militants from Gaza had entered Israel through at least seven locations<ref name="ap1" /> and invaded four small rural Israeli communities, the border city of Sderot, and two military bases from both land and sea.<ref name="nyt7oct" /> Israeli media reported that seven communities came under Hamas control, including [[Nahal Oz]], [[Kfar Aza]], [[Magen, Israel|Magen]], [[Be'eri]], and [[Sufa, Israel|Sufa]].<ref name="guardianlive">{{Cite news |last1=Bayer |first1=Lili |last2=Ho |first2=Vivian |last3=Fulton |first3=Adam |last4=Yang |first4=Maya <!-- author names are changing over time --> |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Israel declares state of war after Hamas fires thousands of rockets and 'militants cross border' – live |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/oct/07/hamas-launches-attack-on-israel-with-5000-rockets-live |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007071116/https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/oct/07/hamas-launches-attack-on-israel-with-5000-rockets-live |url-status=live}}</ref> The [[Erez Crossing]] was reported to have come under Hamas control, enabling militants to enter Israel from Gaza.<ref name="aj7oct" /> Israeli Police Commissioner [[Kobi Shabtai]] said there were 21 active high-confrontation locations in southern Israel.<ref name="jordan1" />

''The New York Times'' reported that an Israeli intelligence document prepared weeks after the attack found that Hamas had breached the border fence in over 30 separate locations.<ref name="nyt-2023-military-gbmoctf">{{cite news |last1=Goldman |first1=Adam |last2=Bergman |first2=Ronen |last3=Mazzetti |first3=Mark |last4=Odenheimer |first4=Natan |last5=Cardia |first5=Alexander |last6=Tiefenthäler |first6=Ainara |last7=Frenkel |first7=Sheera |title=Where Was the Israeli Military? |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/30/world/middleeast/israeli-military-hamas-failures.html |work=[[The New York Times]] |date=December 30, 2023 |access-date=December 30, 2023 |archive-date=December 30, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231230223314/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/30/world/middleeast/israeli-military-hamas-failures.html |url-status=live}}</ref>

Starting at 6.30{{nbsp}}a.m. the same day, [[Nova music festival massacre|a massacre unfolded at an outdoor music festival]] near [[Re'im music festival massacre|Re'im]], resulting in at least 360 dead and many others missing. Witnesses recounted militants on motorcycles opening fire on fleeing participants, who were already dispersing due to rocket fire that had wounded some attendees; some were also taken hostage.<ref Other militants carried out an amphibious [[Battle of Zikim|landing in Zikim]].<ref name="bbc1" /><ref>{{Cite news |last=O'Connor |first=Tom |date=October 7, 2023 |title=What's happening in Israel right now as it battles full-scale Hamas assault |url=https://www.newsweek.com/whats-happening-israel-right-now-it-battles-full-scale-hamas-assault-1832883 |access-date=October 9, 2023 |website=[[Newsweek]] |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008210405/https://www.newsweek.com/whats-happening-israel-right-now-it-battles-full-scale-hamas-assault-1832883 |url-status=live}}</ref> Palestinian sources claim that the local Israeli army base was stormed.<ref>{{Cite web |date=October 9, 2023 |title=This is How Al-Qassam's Navel Units Stormed Zakim's Fortified Military Base – VIDEO |url=https://www.palestinechronicle.com/this-is-how-al-qassams-navel-units-stormed-zakims-fortified-military-base-video/ |access-date=October 9, 2023 |website=Palestine Chronicle |archive-date=October 9, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009212918/https://www.palestinechronicle.com/this-is-how-al-qassams-navel-units-stormed-zakims-fortified-military-base-video/ |url-status=live}}</ref> The IDF said it had killed two attackers on the beach and destroyed four vessels, including two rubber boats. ==== Nova music festival ====
{{main|Nova music festival massacre}}

[[File:Nova massacre dashcam.jpg|thumb|Militant abducting a man during the Re'im music festival massacre that left at least 360 people dead and others taken hostage]]

As part of the Hamas-led attack, 364 civilians were killed and many more wounded at the Supernova Sukkot Gathering, an open-air [[music festival]] celebrating the [[Jewish holidays|Jewish holiday]] of [[Sukkot]] near kibbutz [[Re'im]]. [[Gaza war hostage crisis|At least 40 hostages]] were also taken.<ref>
* {{cite web |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/death-count-from-massacre-at-reim-music-festival-reportedly-updated-to-364-a-third-of-oct-7-deaths/ |title=Death count from Re'im music festival massacre reportedly updated to 364 — a third of Oct. 7 fatalities |work=The Times of Israel |date=November 17, 2023 |access-date=November 20, 2023 |archive-date=November 17, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231117222212/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/death-count-from-massacre-at-reim-music-festival-reportedly-updated-to-364-a-third-of-oct-7-deaths/ |url-status=live}}
* {{cite web |url=https://news.sky.com/story/new-footage-shows-british-israeli-soldier-toss-grenades-back-at-hamas-13008579 |title=New footage shows British-Israeli soldier toss grenades back at Hamas |work=Sky News |date=November 15, 2023 |access-date=November 20, 2023 |archive-date=November 21, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121154502/https://news.sky.com/story/new-footage-shows-british-israeli-soldier-toss-grenades-back-at-hamas-13008579 |url-status=live}}
* {{cite web |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/cpl-liel-vainshtein-19-former-child-star-slain-at-music-festival/ |title=Cpl. Liel Vainshtein, 19: Former child star slain at music festival |work=The Times of Israel |date=October 30, 2023 |access-date=November 20, 2023 |archive-date=November 16, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231116021039/https://www.timesofisrael.com/cpl-liel-vainshtein-19-former-child-star-slain-at-music-festival/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="Gillett">{{cite news |last1=Gillett |first1=Francesca |date=October 8, 2023 |title=How an Israel music festival turned into a nightmare after Hamas attack |agency=[[BBC News]] |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67047034 |url-status=live |access-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008143208/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67047034 |archive-date=October 8, 2023}}</ref><ref name="Tabachnick">{{cite news |last1=Tabachnick |first1=Cara |date=October 8, 2023 |title=Israelis search for loved ones with posts and pleas on social media |work=[[CBS News]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008061931/https://www.cbsnews.com/news/israelis-search-loved-ones-posts-pleas-social-media-hamas-attack/ |archive-date=October 8, 2023}}</ref> This mass killing had the largest number of casualties out of a number of massacres targeting Israeli civilians in communities adjacent to Gaza that were part of the October 7 attack, alongside those at the communities of [[Netiv HaAsara massacre|Netiv HaAsara]], Be'eri, Kfar Aza, Nir Oz, and [[Holit attack|Holit]].<ref>{{Cite news |date=October 10, 2023 |title=Hamas Leaves Trail of Terror in Israel |work=[[The New York Times]] |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/10/world/middleeast/israel-gaza-war-hamas-deaths-killings.html |url-status=live |access-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011163643/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/10/world/middleeast/israel-gaza-war-hamas-deaths-killings.html |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |issn=0362-4331}}</ref>

At 6:30&nbsp;a.m., around sunrise, [[Palestinian rocket attacks on Israel|rockets]] were noticed in the sky. Around 7:00&nbsp;a.m., a siren warned of an incoming rocket attack, prompting festival-goers to flee.<ref>{{Cite web |date=October 8, 2023 |title=Hamas gunmen open fire on hundreds at music festival in southern Israel |work=[[CBS News]] |url=https://www.cbsnews.com/news/hamas-gunmen-open-fire-hundreds-music-festival-southern-israel-kibbutz-reim/ |access-date=October 29, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008062414/https://www.cbsnews.com/news/hamas-gunmen-open-fire-hundreds-music-festival-southern-israel-kibbutz-reim/ |url-status=live}}</ref> Subsequently, armed militants, dressed in military attire and using motorcycles, trucks and powered paragliders, surrounded the festival grounds and indiscriminately fired on people attempting to escape. Attendees seeking refuge nearby, in bomb shelters, bushes, and orchards, were killed while in hiding. Those who reached the road and parking lot were trapped in a traffic jam as militants fired at vehicles. The militants executed some wounded people at point-blank range as they crouched on the ground.<ref>{{Cite news |last1=DeBre |first1=Isabel |last2=Biesecker |first2=Michael |date=October 9, 2023 |title=Israeli survivors recount terror at music festival, where Hamas militants killed at least 260 |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-music-festival-6a55aae2375944f10ecc4c52d05f2ffe |access-date=October 11, 2023 |work=[[Associated Press]] |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011145548/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-music-festival-6a55aae2375944f10ecc4c52d05f2ffe |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="deadly">{{Cite news |date=October 10, 2023 |title=What to know about the deadly Hamas attack on an Israeli music festival |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/10/what-to-know-about-deadly-hamas-attack-on-the-israeli-music-festival |access-date=October 11, 2023 |work=[[Al Jazeera English|Al Jazeera]] |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011170907/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/10/what-to-know-about-deadly-hamas-attack-on-the-israeli-music-festival |url-status=live}}</ref>

The massacre at the festival has been described as the largest terror attack in Israel's history<ref>{{Cite news |last=Debre |first=Isabel |date=October 9, 2023 |title=Israeli survivors recount terror at music festival, where Hamas militants killed at least 260 |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/hamas-attack-music-festival-led-chaos-frantic-attempts-103824517 |access-date=October 11, 2023 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011202607/https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/hamas-attack-music-festival-led-chaos-frantic-attempts-103824517 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>[https://www.economist.com/podcasts/2023/10/09/israel-has-suffered-the-biggest-terror-attack-in-its-history-how-will-it-respond Israel has suffered the biggest terror attack in its history. How will it respond?] {{Webarchive|url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231010034417/https://www.economist.com/podcasts/2023/10/09/israel-has-suffered-the-biggest-terror-attack-in-its-history-how-will-it-respond|date=October 10, 2023}}, [[The Economist]], October 9, 2023</ref><ref name="deadly" /> and the worst Israeli civilian massacre ever.<ref name="RS-Browne">{{Cite magazine |last1=Browne |first1=David |last2=Dillon |first2=Nancy |last3=Grow |first3=Kory |title='They Wanted to Dance in Peace. And They Got Slaughtered'. Israel's Supernova festival celebrated music and unity. It turned into the deadliest concert attack in history |url=https://www.rollingstone.com/music/music-features/hamas-israel-nova-music-festival-massacre-1234854306/ |date=October 15, 2023 |magazine=[[Rolling Stone]] |access-date=October 18, 2023 |archive-date=October 18, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231018015038/https://www.rollingstone.com/music/music-features/hamas-israel-nova-music-festival-massacre-1234854306/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

==== Kfar Aza ====
{{main|Kfar Aza massacre}}

During the Hamas-led attack, around 250 [[Hamas]] militants attacked Kfar Aza, a kibbutz about {{Convert|3|km|mi|sp=us}} from the border with the Gaza Strip, massacring 62 residents and abducting 19 hostages.<ref name=KA />

The kibbutz had more than 950 residents, and it took the IDF nearly three days to wrest back full control of it from militants that fortified themselves in houses of the kibbutz.<ref name=KA>{{Cite news |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/terrorists-took-kfar-aza-in-an-hour-recapturing-it-took-the-idf-days-probe-finds/ |title=Terrorists took Kfar Aza in an hour. Recapturing it took the IDF days, probe finds |first=Emanuel |last=Fabian |date=March 3, 2025 |work=[[Times of Israel]]}}</ref>

==== Be'eri ====
{{main|Be'eri massacre}}

[[File:Gaza envelope after coordinated surprise offensive on Israel, October 2023 (KBG GPO03).jpg|thumb|Blood inside a home in [[Be'eri massacre|Be'eri]]]]

On the morning of the attack, around 70 Hamas militants<ref>{{Cite news |last=Kierszenbaum |first=Quique |date=October 11, 2023 |title='It was a pogrom': Be'eri survivors on the horrific attack by Hamas terrorists |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/11/it-was-a-pogrom-beeri-survivors-horrific-attack-hamas-terrorists |access-date=October 11, 2023 |issn=0261-3077 |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011200820/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/11/it-was-a-pogrom-beeri-survivors-horrific-attack-hamas-terrorists |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |first1=Amanda |last1=Macias |first2=Sam |last2=Meredith |first3=Ruxandra |last3=Iordache |title=Israel-Hamas war live updates: 22 U.S. citizens confirmed dead; Israel to form emergency government |url=https://www.cnbc.com/2023/10/11/live-updates-latest-news-on-gaza-and-israel-hamas-conflict.html |access-date=October 12, 2023 |work=[[CNBC]] |date=October 11, 2023 |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011194235/https://www.cnbc.com/2023/10/11/live-updates-latest-news-on-gaza-and-israel-hamas-conflict.html |url-status=live}}</ref> carried out a massacre at Be'eri, an Israeli kibbutz near the Gaza Strip. At least 130 people were killed in the attack,<ref name="Psyduck (he)" /> including women (such as peace activist [[Vivian Silver]]),<ref>{{Cite news |date=November 13, 2023 |title=Canadian Israeli peace activist Vivian Silver, feared to be held hostage, confirmed killed in Hamas attacks |work=[[CBC News]] |url=https://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/israel-gaza-vivian-silver-1.7027333 |access-date=November 13, 2023 |archive-date=November 13, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231113233658/https://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/israel-gaza-vivian-silver-1.7027333 |url-status=live}}</ref> children, and infants,<ref>{{Cite web |url=https://www.israelhayom.co.il/news/local/article/14679668 |script-title=he:עדויות תושבי העוטף ממתקפת הפתע על ישראל: "טובחים כאן בתינוקות" |title=eduyot toshvi ha'otef memitkafat hafta al yisral: "tovchim kan batinokot" |trans-title=Testimonies from residents of the encirclement from a surprise attack on Israel: "Babies are being slaughtered here" |access-date=October 10, 2023 |work=[[Israel Hayom]] |date=October 7, 2023 |archive-date=October 9, 2023 |language=he |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009173239/https://www.israelhayom.co.il/news/local/article/14679668 |url-status=live}}</ref>{{better source needed|date=December 2024}} claiming the lives of 10% of the community's residents. Dozens of homes were also burned down.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/sktjpy11wt |title='After a minute, my friend was murdered in front of me' |first1=Matan |last1=Tzuri |first2=Roni |last2=Green Shaulov |first3=Adam |last3=Kutub |date=October 9, 2023 |work=[[Ynet]] |access-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-date=October 10, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231010062239/https://www.ynetnews.com/article/sktjpy11wt |url-status=live}}</ref> Several newspapers called the massacre an act of terrorism; some compared the brutality of the atrocities to that of [[Islamic State|ISIS]].<ref>
* {{Cite news |last=Hutchinson |first=Bill |date=October 13, 2023 |title=Israel's 'Ground Zero:' The Be'eri Kibbutz was among the bloodiest scenes of the Hamas attack |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/israels-ground-zero-beeri-kibbutz-bloodiest-scenes-hamas/story?id=103936668 |access-date=November 7, 2023 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]] |archive-date=October 15, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231015025342/https://abcnews.go.com/International/israels-ground-zero-beeri-kibbutz-bloodiest-scenes-hamas/story?id=103936668 |url-status=live}}

==== Psyduck music festival ====
{{Main|Psyduck music festival massacre}}

Psyduck was a small [[trance music]] festival that took place in the open fields near kibbutz [[Nir Oz]], about {{convert|2|km|mi}} from the border of [[Gaza Strip|Gaza]]. The event drew around 100 participants. Hamas militants attacked the festival, killing 17 [[Israelis]]. Some were fatally shot at the festival site, while others were killed as they attempted to escape to nearby kibbutzim. Most survivors hid under small bushes until Israel Defense Forces rescued them a few hours later.<ref name="Psyduck (he)" >{{Cite news |last=שמעוני |first=מור |date=December 1, 2023 |script-title=he:"כשעלה הבוקר התחיל מטח, כל אחד רץ למקום אחר" {{!}} הטבח במסיבה המחתרתית |language=he |trans-title=When morning came, a barrage of rockets started and everyone scattered {{!}} The massacre at the underground party |work=[[Ynet]] |url=https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/hkdnxour6 |access-date=December 18, 2023 |archive-date=December 18, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231218202448/https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/hkdnxour6 |url-status=live}}</ref>

==== Nir Am ====
[[Nir Am]] was attacked but no residents were harmed. [[Inbal Rabin-Lieberman]], the 25-year-old security coordinator, alongside her uncle Ami, led a guard detail that killed multiple militants attempting to infiltrate a nearby chicken farm. They successfully deterred the rest of the invading militants from entering the community.<ref name="ToI10oct2023">{{cite news |title=In Ofakim, one woman's graceful bravery offers precious solace to a grieving nation |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/in-ofakim-one-womans-graceful-bravery-offers-precious-solace-to-a-grieving-nation/ |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |access-date=October 13, 2023 |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011143848/https://www.timesofisrael.com/in-ofakim-one-womans-graceful-bravery-offers-precious-solace-to-a-grieving-nation/ |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="Haaretz11oct2023">{{cite news |title=Israeli Woman Who Helped Save a Kibbutz: 'I'm Not a Hero, I Wasn't There by Myself' |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-11/ty-article/.premium/israeli-woman-who-helped-save-a-kibbutz-im-not-a-hero-i-wasnt-there-by-myself/0000018b-1e4f-d47b-a7fb-bfdf2e560000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |first=Ran |last=Shimoni |date=October 11, 2023 |access-date=October 13, 2023 |archive-date=October 13, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231013003223/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-11/ty-article/.premium/israeli-woman-who-helped-save-a-kibbutz-im-not-a-hero-i-wasnt-there-by-myself/0000018b-1e4f-d47b-a7fb-bfdf2e560000 |url-status=live}}</ref>

==== Ofakim ====
{{main|Battle of Ofakim}}

In the town of Ofakim, 47 were people killed in the October 7, attacks.<ref name= "toi Golan Druze">{{Cite news |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/daily-briefing-jul-29-day-297-golans-druze-demand-reprisal-for-12-killed-by-hezbollah/ |title=Daily Briefing Jul 29: Day 297 – Golan's Druze demand reprisal for 12 killed by Hezbollah |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |access-date=August 24, 2024 |archive-date=August 1, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240801223258/https://www.timesofisrael.com/daily-briefing-jul-29-day-297-golans-druze-demand-reprisal-for-12-killed-by-hezbollah/ |url-status=live}}</ref> [[Ofakim]] was the furthest point reached by the initial intense attacks on October 7. A large proportion of the population of the town is working-class Jews of North African descent.<ref name="AP - Ofakim">{{cite news |title=DIARY: Under siege by Hamas militants, a hometown and the lives within it are scarred forever |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-hamas-militants-attack-cec3cc9e14969fd100d342ad1b90f7e4 |access-date=July 7, 2024 |work=[[Associated Press]] |date=October 20, 2023 |language=en}}</ref> Ofakim was one of the first locations where a "hostages situation" was reported.<ref name="CNN Ofakim" >{{cite news |last1=Dahman |first1=Ibrahim |last2=Gold |first2=Hadas |last3=Iszo |first3=Lauren |last4=Tal |first4=Amir |last5=Salman |first5=Abeer |last6=Khadder |first6=Kareem |last7=Greene |first7=Richard Allen |last8=Alam |first8=Hande Atay |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Netanyahu says Israel is 'at war' after Hamas launches surprise attack, takes hostages |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/07/middleeast/sirens-israel-rocket-attack-gaza-intl-hnk/index.html |access-date=July 8, 2024 |work=[[CNN]] |language=en |quote=Another IDF spokesman, Brigadier General Daniel Hagari, said there were hostage situations in two locations – Ofakim and Beeri. |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007094105/https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/07/middleeast/sirens-israel-rocket-attack-gaza-intl-hnk/index.html |url-status=live}}</ref> The militants targeted the parts of the town where the housing was older and did not have individual bomb shelters in every home, and locals reported that the invaders had shot people who were trying to get to communal shelters.<ref name="Haaretz - Ofakim 8 Oct">{{cite news |title=The Israeli Town of Ofakim Has Been Cleared of Terrorists but the Blood and Shock Remain |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-08/ty-article-magazine/.premium/the-israeli-town-of-ofakim-has-been-cleared-of-terrorists-but-the-blood-and-shock-remain/0000018b-0fe0-dfff-a7eb-aff8ad030000 |access-date=July 7, 2024 |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=October 8, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008183420/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-08/ty-article-magazine/.premium/the-israeli-town-of-ofakim-has-been-cleared-of-terrorists-but-the-blood-and-shock-remain/0000018b-0fe0-dfff-a7eb-aff8ad030000 |url-status=live}}</ref>

==== Rahat ====

A number of Qassam Brigades militants infiltrated the [[Bedouin]] city of [[Rahat]], north-east of [[Ofakim]] and 30 kilometres from Gaza, representing the furthest extent of the incursions by Palestinian militant groups on October 7. Over a month after the initial attack, two militants were arrested by Israeli police.<ref name="toi - Rahat" >{{cite news |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/report-2-gaza-terrorists-found-in-rahat-a-month-after-october-7-assault/ |title=2 Gaza terrorists found in Rahat a month after October 7 assault |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |access-date=June 18, 2024 |archive-date=April 20, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240420074838/https://www.timesofisrael.com/report-2-gaza-terrorists-found-in-rahat-a-month-after-october-7-assault/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

=== Failed plans ===
A Hamas group carried intelligence information and maps guiding it to the border of the West Bank, suggesting it had intentions of going all the way to the West Bank.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2023/11/12/hamas-planning-terror-gaza-israel/ |title=Hamas envisioned deeper attacks, aiming to provoke an Israeli war |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |date=November 12, 2023 |author=Shira Rubin and Joby Warrick |access-date=February 21, 2024 |archive-date=November 13, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231113024604/http://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2023/11/12/hamas-planning-terror-gaza-israel/ |url-status=live}}</ref>

According to a report in [[Asharq Al-Awsat]], two Hamas units had plans of reaching [[Shikma Prison]] in [[Ashkelon]] (13&nbsp;km from the Gaza Strip) with the aim of freeing Palestinian inmates. One cell got lost and ended up in [[Sderot]], at which point they were told to change their plans and operate in Sderot. A second cell which was operating in [[Zikim]] was commanded to go up to Ashkelon, but the cell was completely gunned down by Israeli security forces in Zikim.<ref>{{cite news |url= https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-planned-ashkelon-jail-raid-to-free-palestinian-prisoners-on-october-7-report/|title= Hamas planned Ashkelon jail raid to free Palestinian prisoners on October 7 – report|newspaper=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=February 20, 2024 |author= |access-date=May 3, 2025 |archive-date=February 21, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240221033444/https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-planned-ashkelon-jail-raid-to-free-palestinian-prisoners-on-october-7-report/|url-status=live}}</ref>

=== Hostages taken ===
{{main|Gaza war hostage crisis}}

[[File:Hamas gunmen capturing civilian hostages.png|thumb|Hamas gunmen with civilian hostages.]]
Soon after the start of the Hamas operation, there were reports that many civilians and soldiers had been taken as captives back to the Gaza Strip. Later in the day Hamas announced it had captured enough Israeli soldiers to force a [[prisoner swap]],<ref name=":16" /> and Israel confirmed hostages had been taken.<ref name=cnbc>{{Cite news |url=https://www.cnbc.com/2023/10/07/israel-declares-state-of-war-alert-after-surprise-hamas-attack.html |title=Israel vows 'mighty vengeance' after deadliest day in 50 years following surprise Hamas attack |date=October 7, 2023 |work=[[CNBC]] |access-date=December 19, 2023 |archive-date=December 19, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231219030130/https://www.cnbc.com/2023/10/07/israel-declares-state-of-war-alert-after-surprise-hamas-attack.html |url-status=live}}</ref><!-- Hamas had captured ~12 IDF soldiers including 6 women, 6 men living men, along with the bodies of 6 IDF soldiers who died on October 7.{{citation needed|reason=19 is the total from the list in Haaretz, I need to double check how many men were alive.}} They also already had captured two male IDF soldier on in 2014 who had not returned, at least one of these men is dead, Hamas and the IDF dispute the status of the other.{{citation needed|reason=same citation as previously, plus the man Hamas claim is still alive has a Wiki page אורון שאול Oron Shaul.}} -->

In Be'eri, up to 50 people were taken hostage; after an 18-hour standoff between militants and IDF forces, they were freed.<ref name="BBChostage">{{cite news |last=Davies |first=Alys |date=October 8, 2023 |title=What we know about Israeli hostages taken by Hamas |publisher=[[BBC News]] |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67044255 |url-status=live |access-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008025612/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67044255 |archive-date=October 8, 2023}}</ref> Hostages were also reported taken in [[Ofakim]], where policemen led by [[Israel Police#Ranks|Chief Superintendent]] [[Jayar Davidov]] engaged Palestinian militants in a shootout on October 7; Davidov and three of his men were killed, and the IDF later rescued two Israeli hostages in the suburb of [[Urim, Israel|Urim]].<ref name="BBChostage" /><ref>{{cite news |title=ג'יי אר דוידוב, מפקד משטרת רהט, נהרג בקרב ליד אופקים |url=https://www.mako.co.il/men-men_news/Article-6a787420aab0b81027.htm |access-date=May 19, 2025 |publisher=Mako |date=October 7, 2025 |language=he}}</ref> There were reports of militants killing and stealing family pets.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Leshem |first=Eitan |date=October 14, 2023 |title="הם היו בבית 3–4 ימים, חלקם בלי אוכל, חלקם לבד, לא מעט מהם הגיעו אלינו רועדים": הזוועה לא פסחה על חיות המחמד |language=he |trans-title=They were in their houses for 3–4 days, some of them without food, some of them alone, quite a few of them came to us trembling: The horror did not spare the pets |work=[[Haaretz]] |url=https://www.haaretz.co.il/travel/2023-10-14/ty-article/.premium/0000018b-22e4-dd34-afdf-f7e79ac30000 |access-date=October 14, 2023 |archive-date=October 20, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231020003819/https://www.haaretz.co.il/travel/2023-10-14/ty-article/.premium/0000018b-22e4-dd34-afdf-f7e79ac30000 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Hamas took many hostages back to Gaza. On October 16, they said they were holding 250 hostages<ref>{{Cite news |last=Sherwood |first=Harriet |date=October 17, 2023 |title=Hamas says 250 people held hostage in Gaza |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/16/israeli-hostages-hamas-gaza |access-date=October 17, 2023 |issn=0261-3077 |archive-date=October 16, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016235352/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/16/israeli-hostages-hamas-gaza |url-status=live}}</ref> and that it had done so to force Israel to release its Palestinian prisoners.<ref name="aj9">{{cite news |title=Hamas says it has enough Israeli captives to free all Palestinian prisoners |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]] |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/hamas-says-it-has-enough-israeli-captives-to-free-all-palestinian-prisoners |url-status=live |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007163709/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/hamas-says-it-has-enough-israeli-captives-to-free-all-palestinian-prisoners |archive-date=October 7, 2023}}</ref> In addition to hostages with only Israeli citizenship, almost half of the hostages were foreign nationals or held [[multiple citizenship]]s.<ref>{{Cite news |date=October 25, 2023 |title=More than half of Hamas' hostages have foreign nationality – Israel |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/more-than-half-hamas-hostages-have-foreign-nationality-israel-2023-10-25/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231106003621/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/more-than-half-hamas-hostages-have-foreign-nationality-israel-2023-10-25/ |archive-date=November 6, 2023 |access-date=November 6, 2023 |publisher=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> Some hostages were [[Negev Bedouin]]s.<ref name=":53">{{Cite news |date=October 17, 2023 |title=Israel's Negev Bedouins, forgotten victims of the Hamas attack, rally to provide aid |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20231017-negev-bedouins-israel-s-forgotten-victims-of-the-hamas-attack-rally-to-provide-aid |access-date=April 25, 2024 |work=[[France 24]] |archive-date=April 22, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240422233135/https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20231017-negev-bedouins-israel-s-forgotten-victims-of-the-hamas-attack-rally-to-provide-aid |url-status=live }}</ref> Some of the hostages, including three members of the [[Kidnapping of the Bibas family|Bibas family]], were subsequently handed over to other militant groups.<!-- pre prepared with tips on finding these refs for if I'm not back in a couple of hours {{citation needed| reason = there are several on that pages and it's associated talk page, please copy them here. }} --> [[Palestinian Islamic Jihad]] ended up holding at least 30 of the hostages, but it is unclear whether they or Hamas originally kidnapped them. <!-- incase I forget to follow up {{citation needed| reason = there are plenty available, the 30+ stat is from a Human Rights Watch report condemning PIJ and Hamas for war crimes. }} -->

According to [[Ariel Merari]], the raiders "were ordered to kidnap as many [people] as possible... [and] they intentionally kidnapped a populace that is sensitive from the aspect of Israeli public opinion".<ref name="Merari 2023-11-12">{{Cite interview |last=מררי |first=אריאל |interviewer=ליאור קודנר |title=פרופ' אריאל מררי: אין לי ספק – חמאס חטף תינוקות כדי להתגונן ממתקפה ישראלית |url=https://www.haaretz.co.il/digital/podcast/weekly/2023-11-12/ty-article-podcast/0000018b-c36d-dc2b-a3fb-e7fd61560000 |date=November 12, 2023 |access-date=November 13, 2023 |archive-date=November 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231112174140/https://www.haaretz.co.il/digital/podcast/weekly/2023-11-12/ty-article-podcast/0000018b-c36d-dc2b-a3fb-e7fd61560000 |url-status=live }}</ref>
