The total number killed during the attack is 1,219,<ref name="marks"/> of whom at least 379 were from [[Israeli security forces]] and at least 810 were civilians<ref name="at1189"/> (including 71 foreign).<ref name="F24231215"/> 26.6% of those killed were female.<ref name="aoav_gender"/> Initially up to 1,400 people were reported killed; on November 10, this was revised to 1,200,<ref name="barrons.com">{{Cite web |url=https://www.barrons.com/news/israel-revises-down-october-7-hamas-attack-death-toll-to-1-200-foreign-ministry-07097f94 |title=Israel Revises Down October 7 Hamas Attack Death Toll To 1,200: Foreign Ministry |website=[[Barron's]] |access-date=November 10, 2023 |archive-date=November 10, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231110195126/https://www.barrons.com/news/israel-revises-down-october-7-hamas-attack-death-toll-to-1-200-foreign-ministry-07097f94 |url-status=live}}</ref> before being revised further in December. The casualties included 38 children;<ref name="38children"/> the youngest person killed was 10 months old,<ref name="F24231215"/> and 25 were over age 80.<ref name="toi_casulties"/> The attack was the deadliest day in Israel's history.<ref>{{Cite news |date=October 7, 2024 |title=Hamas terrorist attacks on October 7: The deadliest day in Israel's history |url=https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20241007-hamas-terrorist-attacks-7-october-deadliest-day-israel-history-anniversary |access-date=February 3, 2025 |work=[[France 24]] |language=en}}</ref> According to the Center for Strategic and International Studies, the attack is the deadliest per capita terrorist attack.<ref name=":4">{{Cite web|url=https://www.csis.org/analysis/hamass-october-7-attack-visualizing-data|title=Hamas's October 7 Attack: Visualizing the Data|date=2023-12-19|access-date=2025-12-01|website=Center for Strategic and International Studies|last=Byman|first=Daniel|last2=McCabe|first2=Riley|last3=Palmer|first3=Alexander|last4=Doxsee|first4=Catrina|last5=Holtz|first5=Mackenzie|last6=Duff|first6=Delaney|quote=The October 7 attack is the deadliest per capita terrorist attack since the [[Global Terrorism Database]] started data collection in 1970, with a rate of slightly over one person killed per every 10,000 Israelis.}}</ref> Some, including then-US President Joe Biden, have said it was also the deadliest day for Jews since the Holocaust.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Staff |date=October 12, 2023 |title=Hamas attack 'deadliest day for Jews since the Holocaust', says Biden, as Israeli jets pound Gaza |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/12/israel-hamas-war-biden-jews-holocaust-palestine-iran-warning |access-date=February 3, 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |issn=0261-3077}}</ref> Others such as historian [[Enzo Traverso]] and Holocaust and Genocide scholar [[Raz Segal]] have warned against invoking the Holocaust in relation to October 7.<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Confavreux |first1=Josep |last2=Dejean |first2=Mathieu |date=November 5, 2023 |title=Enzo Traverso : la guerre à Gaza « brouille la mémoire de l'Holocauste » |trans-title=Enzo Traverso: Gaza war 'blurs memory of Holocaust' |url=https://www.mediapart.fr/journal/international/051123/enzo-traverso-la-guerre-gaza-brouille-la-memoire-de-l-holocauste |access-date=February 3, 2025 |website=Mediapart |language=fr}}</ref><ref name=segal>{{Cite news |last=Segal |first=Raz |author-link=Raz Segal |date=October 24, 2023 |title=Israel must stop weaponising the Holocaust |url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2023/oct/24/israel-gaza-palestinians-holocaust |access-date=February 3, 2025 |work=[[The Guardian]] |language=en-GB |issn=0261-3077}}</ref> Segal condemned the "weaponizations of Holocaust memory" by Biden, Israeli politicians and others, saying it is done "not in order to stand with powerless people facing the prospect of genocidal violence, but to support and justify an extremely violent attack by a powerful state and, at the same time, distort this reality."<ref name=segal />

The attack left over 3,400 wounded,<ref name="cas2,2">{{cite news |title=Israeli death toll from Hamas attack surpasses 1,000, top military officer says |url=https://thehill.com/policy/4247805-israeli-death-toll-from-hamas-attack-surpasses-1000-top-military-officer-says/ |access-date=October 10, 2023 |work=[[The Hill (newspaper)|The Hill]] |date=October 10, 2023 |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011133836/https://thehill.com/policy/4247805-israeli-death-toll-from-hamas-attack-surpasses-1000-top-military-officer-says/ |url-status=live}}</ref> and 247 soldiers and civilians were taken hostage.<ref name="Isrcaptured" /> On October 19, Israeli officials reported an additional 100 to 200 missing.<ref name="IsrMIA">{{cite news|url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-19/ty-article/.premium/israel-believes-some-of-those-missing-after-hamas-attack-will-not-be-found/0000018b-4942-d5d2-afef-cdff5b7f0000|title=Israel Believes Some of Those Missing After Hamas' Attack Will Not Be Found|work=Haaretz|first=Yaniv|last=Kubovich|date=October 19, 2023|access-date=October 20, 2023|archive-date=October 20, 2023|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231020001636/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-19/ty-article/.premium/israel-believes-some-of-those-missing-after-hamas-attack-will-not-be-found/0000018b-4942-d5d2-afef-cdff5b7f0000|url-status=live}}</ref> By July 2024, the number of missing was down to 1.<ref name="missing"/> Israeli casualties include about 70 [[Arab citizens of Israel|Arab Israelis]], predominantly from [[Negev Bedouin]] communities.<ref>
* {{Cite web |last=Johnston |first=Holly |date=October 12, 2023 |title=Palestinian paramedic missing after Hamas attack at Israel music festival |url=https://www.thenationalnews.com/mena/2023/10/12/paramedic-missing-hamas-attack-israel-music-festival/ |access-date=October 12, 2023 |website=The National |archive-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231012180504/https://www.thenationalnews.com/mena/2023/10/12/paramedic-missing-hamas-attack-israel-music-festival/ |url-status=live}}

* {{Cite news |title=At least six Arab Israelis missing since Hamas attack, likely kidnapped |work=[[Haaretz]] |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-10/ty-article-live/900-israelis-killed-2-400-wounded-in-war-with-hamas/0000018b-17bd-d465-abbb-17bf23000000 |access-date=October 11, 2023 |first1=Jack |last1=Khoury |first2=Nir |last2=Hasson |date=October 10, 2023 |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011013109/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-10/ty-article-live/900-israelis-killed-2-400-wounded-in-war-with-hamas/0000018b-17bd-d465-abbb-17bf23000000 |url-status=live}}</ref> The attack affected a province with a population of 4,000,000 Israelis, while the war displaced 300,000 Israelis.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://go.ifrc.org/emergencies/6678/details |title=Israel – Complex Emergency |newspaper=IFRC |date= |author= |access-date=January 21, 2024}}</ref>

On October 7, over 100 civilians were killed in the [[Be'eri massacre]], including women and children, and over 270 people were killed at a [[Re'im music festival massacre|music festival in Re'im]].<ref name=Testimony-fr/> As of October 10, over 100 people had been reported killed in the [[Kfar Aza massacre]], with the total death toll unknown.<ref name=":5">{{Cite web|title=Corpses and kid's bikes, burned homes and death in kibbutz where Hamas butchered Nine people were fatally shot at a bus shelter in Sderot.<ref name="ap1" /> At least four people were reported killed in [[Kuseife]].<ref name="aj7oct" /> At least 400 wounded were treated in Ashkelon,<ref>{{cite news|title='Nobody could help us' – Shock and anger in Israel's Ashkelon|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67048672 |access-date=October 9, 2023|publisher=[[BBC News]]|date=October 8, 2023 |archive-date=October 9, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009000452/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67048672 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="cnn1" /> while 280 others were reported in Beer Sheva, 60 of whom were in serious condition.<ref name="ap1" /> In the north, injuries from rocket attacks were reported in Tel Aviv.<ref>{{cite news|last=Sella|first=Adam|date=October 8, 2023|title=Tel Aviv's residents start venturing out|publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]]|url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/8/tel-avivs-resident-start-venturing-out |url-status=live |access-date=October 10, 2023 children and adolescents under the age of 19 were killed in the attack.<ref>{{cite news |title=14 kids under 10, 25 people over 80: Up-to-date breakdown of Oct 7 victims we know about |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/14-kids-under-10-25-people-over-80-up-to-date-breakdown-of-oct-7-victims-we-know-about/ |work=The Times of Israel |date=December 4, 2023 |access-date=December 15, 2023 |archive-date=December 4, 2023 [[File:120275 memorial site - reim forest PikiWiki Israel.jpg|thumb|Israelis killed during Re'im music festival massacre]]
The great number and geographical spread of the victims made locating all of their remains difficult. Several weeks after the massacre, once conventional [[Search and rescue|search techniques]] had been exhausted, the IDF approached the [[Israel Nature and Parks Authority]] for help in [[Wildlife radio telemetry|tracking]] the flight paths of vultures, which resulted in the discovery of at least five more bodies.<ref>{{Cite news |last=לשם |first=איתן |date=November 8, 2023 |title=צה"ל משתמש במשדרים המוצמדים לעופות דורסים כדי לאתר גופות נסתרות בשטח |language=he |work=Haaretz |url=https://www.haaretz.co.il/travel/2023-11-08/ty-article/.premium/0000018b-a3f9-dc0b-a1cb-e7fffd970000 |access-date=November 9, 2023}}</ref> The IDF also enlisted the aid of archaeologists from the [[Israel Antiquities Authority]] to help recover remains that were so badly burned as to be indistinguishable from the surrounding rubble; the remains of at least ten victims have been recovered this way.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Gritten |first=David |date=November 7, 2023 |title=Israeli archaeologists help find remains of Hamas attack victims|publisher=[[BBC News]] |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67343928 |access-date=November 12, 2023 |archive-date=November 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231112111142/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67343928 |url-status=live }}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last1=Lubell |first1=Maayan |last2=Hayun |first2=Dedi |date=November 8, 2023 |title=Israeli archaeologists help find remains of Hamas attack victims |publisher=Reuters |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-archaeologists-help-find-remains-hamas-attack-victims-2023-11-08/ |access-date=November 12, 2023 |archive-date=November 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231112111142/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-archaeologists-help-find-remains-hamas-attack-victims-2023-11-08/ |url-status=live }}</ref>

Hamas took at least 247 people hostage and transported them to Gaza.<ref name="Isrcaptured" /> On October 8, [[Palestinian Islamic Jihad]] said it was holding at least 30 captives.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Pacchiani|first1=Gianluca|title=Islamic Jihad leader claims terror group is holding over 30 Israeli hostages|url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/islamic-jihad-leader-claims-terror-group-is-holding-over-30-israeli-hostages/|access-date=October 8, 2023|work=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=October 8, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008184608/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/islamic-jihad-leader-claims-terror-group-is-holding-over-30-israeli-hostages/ |url-status=live}}</ref> At least four people were reportedly taken from Kfar Aza.<ref name="ap3">{{cite news |last1=Goldenberg |first1=Tia |last2=Shurafa |first2=Wafaa |date=October 8, 2023 |title=Hamas fighters storm Israeli towns in surprise attack; Israel responds with deadly strikes on Gaza |publisher=[[Associated Press]] |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-ca7903976387cfc1e1011ce9ea805a71 |url-status=live |access-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008051308/https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-gaza-hamas-rockets-airstrikes-tel-aviv-ca7903976387cfc1e1011ce9ea805a71 |archive-date=October 8, 2023}}</ref> Videos from Gaza appeared to show captured people, with Gazan residents cheering trucks carrying dead bodies.<ref name="nyt7oct" /> Four captives were later reported to have been killed in Be'eri,<ref>{{Cite news|title=Civilian hostages in Hamas custody killed in Be'eri near Gaza border, CNN verified videos show |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/09/middleeast/israel-gaza-hamas-beeri-hostages-killed-intl-hnk/index.html |access-date=October 9, 2023 |publisher=[[CNN]] |archive-date=October 9, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009082701/https://edition.cnn.com/2023/10/09/middleeast/israel-gaza-hamas-beeri-hostages-killed-intl-hnk/index.html |url-status=live}}</ref> while Hamas said that an IDF airstrike on Gaza on October 9 killed four captives.<ref>{{Cite news|title=Israeli Strikes On Gaza Kill Four 'Prisoners': Hamas|url=https://www.barrons.com/news/israeli-strikes-on-gaza-kill-four-prisoners-hamas-76bea3c9?refsec=topics_afp-news |access-date=October 9, 2023|work=[[Barron's]] |archive-date=October 9, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231009130842/https://www.barrons.com/news/israeli-strikes-on-gaza-kill-four-prisoners-hamas-76bea3c9?refsec=topics_afp-news |url-status=live}}</ref> ''[[Yedioth Ahronoth]]'' photographer [[Roy Edan]] was reported missing and likely captured alongside his child in Kfar Aza. His wife was killed and two of their children were able to hide in a closet until rescued.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/sjsninbzp|title=Ynet Photographer missing with daughter, wife murdered |first1=Matan |last1=Tzuri |first2=Lior |last2=El-Hai |date=October 9, 2023 |work=[[Ynet]] |access-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231012210310/https://www.ynetnews.com/article/sjsninbzp|url-status=live}}</ref> Edan's body was identified ten days later as one of the casualties of the [[Kfar Aza massacre]].<ref>{{Cite web |last= |first= |title=צלם ynet רועי עידן נרצח בכפר עזה עם אשתו, הבת הקטנה נעדרת, "חבר טוב ואדם מיוחד ויקר" |url=https://www.inn.co.il/news/617228 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231019214559/https://www.inn.co.il/news/617228 |archive-date=October 19, 2023 |access-date=October 19, 2023 |website=inn.co.il |language=he}}</ref> American-Israeli Hersh Goldberg-Polin [[Kidnapping of Hersh Goldberg-Polin|was one of the kidnapped]]. On October 11, Hamas's Qassam Brigades released a video appearing to show the release of three hostages, a woman and two children, in an open area near a fence. Israel dismissed the video as "theatrics".<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/11/hamas-video-appears-to-show-release-of-woman-two-children |title=Hamas video appears to show release of woman, two children |date=October 11, 2023 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]] |access-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231012192501/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/11/hamas-video-appears-to-show-release-of-woman-two-children |url-status=live}}</ref> According to [[Ynet]], there were also casualties from [[friendly fire]] on October 7 which the IDF believed "it would not be morally sound to investigate [...] due to the immense and complex quantity of them that took place in the kibbutzim and southern Israeli communities due to the challenging situations the soldiers were in at the time."<ref name="YnetFF">{{cite news |last=Zitun |first=Yoav |date=December 12, 2023 |title=One-fifth of troop fatalities in Gaza due to friendly fire or accidents, IDF reports |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/rkjqoobip |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231214212217/https://www.ynetnews.com/article/rkjqoobip |archive-date=December 14, 2023 |access-date=December 15, 2023 |work=[[Ynetnews]] |quote=Casualties fell as a result of friendly fire on October 7, but the IDF believes that beyond the operational investigations of the events, it would not be morally sound to investigate these incidents due to the immense and complex quantity of them that took place in the kibbutzim and southern Israeli communities due to the challenging situations the soldiers were in at the time.}}</ref>

===Identification of remains===
[[File:Disaster Victim Identification after 2023 Hamas attack on Israel (ZAKA1049)..jpg|thumb|According to [[Chen Kugel]], head of the [[Abu Kabir Forensic Institute]], hundreds of bodies arrived at the institute in a state "beyond recognition"]]
According to [[Chen Kugel]], head of the [[Abu Kabir Forensic Institute]], hundreds of bodies arrived at the institute in a state "beyond recognition".<ref name=":4a">{{Cite news |last=ראובני |first=נוב |date=October 24, 2023 |title=חשבו שהם ראו כבר הכל: אנשי המכון לרפואה משפטית מדברים על הזוועות |work=כאן 11 |url=https://www.kan.org.il/content/kan/kan-actual/p-11894/news-item/581538/ |access-date=October 27, 2023 |archive-date=October 26, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026235158/https://www.kan.org.il/content/kan/kan-actual/p-11894/news-item/581538/ |url-status=live }}</ref> Pathologists were required to process, among others, bone fragments recovered from fires; a blood-soaked [[Infant bed|baby mattress]]; victims who were tied, then executed; and two victims who were tied, then incinerated alive.<ref name=":4a" />

With hundreds missing and bodies burned beyond recognition, Israeli authorities assembled recovery teams from across society. This included archaeologists from the [[Israel Antiquities Authority]], who identified and removed ancient remains in attempts to sift through ash and rubble for bone fragments other forensic teams overlooked.<ref name="arch">{{cite news
|url=https://www.economist.com/1843/2023/11/05/the-biblical-archaeologist-finding-the-victims-hamas-burned
|title=The biblical archaeologist finding the victims Hamas burned
|newspaper=[[The Economist]]
|first=Wendell
|last=Steavenson
|date=November 5, 2023
|access-date=November 6, 2023
|archive-date=November 7, 2023
|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107105307/https://www.economist.com/1843/2023/11/05/the-biblical-archaeologist-finding-the-victims-hamas-burned
|url-status=live
}}</ref>

The sheer number of casualties overwhelmed authorities. Bodies were brought chaotically to the Shura IDF base and Abu Kabir forensic institute. The different military, police, and civilian teams caused confusion. Archeologists systematically searched rooms, dividing them into grids and carefully extracting bone shards. At one house, the archeology team found a bloodstain under ash that it determined was the outline of a body, later identified by DNA analysis as Meni Godard.<ref name="arch"/>

At the end of May 2024, using social security data, this was further revised to 1,189: 810 civilians (including 71 foreign nationals) and 379 [[Israeli security forces|security forces]].<ref name="F24231215"/><ref name="at1189"/> One person,<ref>[https://www.barrons.com/news/new-tally-puts-october-7-attack-dead-in-israel-at-1-163-78182279 New Tally Puts October 7 Attack Dead In Israel At 1,163] {{Webarchive|url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240303000937/https://www.barrons.com/news/new-tally-puts-october-7-attack-dead-in-israel-at-1-163-78182279 |date=March 3, 2024 }}</ref> peace activist Bilha Inon, was classed as missing<ref name="missing">{{Cite web|url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/netanyahu-pleads-ignorance-in-meeting-with-families-of-slain-surveillance-soldiers/|title=Netanyahu pleads ignorance in meeting with families of slain surveillance soldiers &#124; The Times of Israel|website=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=July 17, 2024 |access-date=July 17, 2024|archive-date=July 17, 2024|archive-url=https://archive.today/20240717101017/https://www.timesofisrael.com/netanyahu-pleads-ignorance-in-meeting-with-families-of-slain-surveillance-soldiers/|url-status=live}}</ref> until August 6, 2024, when the IDF confirmed that she died at Netiv Ha'asara, with her husband.<ref>{{Cite web|last1=Fabian |first1=Emanuel |last2=Spiro |first2=Amy |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/final-unaccounted-for-october-7-victim-died-in-onslaught-idf-confirms/|title=Final unaccounted for October 7 victim died in onslaught, IDF confirms &#124; The Times of Israel|website=[[The Times of Israel]] |date=August 6, 2024 |access-date=August 8, 2024|archive-date=August 8, 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240808100734/https://www.timesofisrael.com/final-unaccounted-for-october-7-victim-died-in-onslaught-idf-confirms/|url-status=live}}</ref>

== Reported atrocities ==
{{See also|Bearing Witness (2023 film)|War crimes in the Gaza war}}

=== Sexual violence ===
{{Main|Sexual and gender-based violence in the October 7 attacks}}

Israeli women and girls were reportedly raped, assaulted, and mutilated by Hamas militants during the incursion, an allegation Hamas denies.<ref name="NYTrapeinvestigation"/><ref name="Associated Press-2023">{{cite news |date=December 6, 2023 |title=Biden calls reports of Hamas raping Israeli hostages 'appalling,' says world can't look away |publisher=[[Associated Press]] |url=https://apnews.com/article/biden-hamas-rape-israel-sexual-violence-155Jq5pu3245d4418M19YnRvau7Rc14hVB}}</ref><ref>

* {{cite news |title=Sexual Violence Evidence Against Hamas Is Mounting, but the Road to Court Is Still Long |work=[[Haaretz]] |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-22/ty-article-magazine/.premium/sexual-assault-evidence-against-hamas-is-mounting-but-the-road-to-court-is-still-long/0000018b-f6bb-dafe-a18f-f7fb0a570000 |url-status=live |access-date=November 29, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231123215829/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-22/ty-article-magazine/.premium/sexual-assault-evidence-against-hamas-is-mounting-but-the-road-to-court-is-still-long/0000018b-f6bb-dafe-a18f-f7fb0a570000 |archive-date=November 23, 2023}}
* {{Cite news |title=The Scope of Hamas' Campaign of Rape Against Israeli Women Is Revealed, Testimony After Testimony |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-30/ty-article-magazine/.highlight/hamas-campaign-of-rape-against-israeli-women-is-revealed-testimony-after-testimony/0000018c-2144-da36-a1de-6767dac90000 |archive-date=January 7, 2024 |access-date=February 5, 2024 |work=Haaretz}}</ref> In the months following the attacks, ''[[The Wall Street Journal]]'' reported on December 21, there was "mounting evidence of [[sexual violence]], based on survivor accounts, first responders and witnesses."<ref name="WSJ 12-21">{{cite news |last1=Stancati |first1=Margherita |last2=Ayyoub |first2=Abeer |date=December 21, 2023 |title=Gazans Are Starting to Blame Hamas for Wartime Suffering |url=https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/gazans-are-starting-to-blame-hamas-for-wartime-suffering-066256b0 |url-access=subscription |url-status=live |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231221041400/https://www.wsj.com/world/middle-east/gazans-are-starting-to-blame-hamas-for-wartime-suffering-066256b0 |archive-date=December 21, 2023 |access-date=December 21, 2023 |work=[[The Wall Street Journal]]}}</ref> Critics of Hamas denounced what they said was gender-based violence, war crimes, and crimes against humanity.<ref>{{cite news |last=Lawless |first=Jill |agency=[[Associated Press]] |date=November 5, 2023 |title=How international law applies to war, and why Hamas and Israel are both alleged to have broken it |url=https://www.latimes.com/world-nation/story/2023-11-05/how-international-law-applies-to-war-and-why-hamas-and-israel-are-both-alleged-to-have-broken-it |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231128175241/https://www.latimes.com/world-nation/story/2023-11-05/how-international-law-applies-to-war-and-why-hamas-and-israel-are-both-alleged-to-have-broken-it |archive-date=November 28, 2023 |access-date=November 29, 2023 |work=[[Los Angeles Times]]}}</ref><ref name="BBC News-2023">{{cite news |date=December 5, 2023 |title=Israel Gaza: Hamas raped and mutilated women on 7 October, BBC hears |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67629181 |publisher=[[BBC News]] |access-date=December 7, 2023}}</ref>

The BBC reported that "Videos of naked and bloodied women filmed by Hamas on the day of the attack, and photographs of bodies taken at the sites afterwards, suggest that women were sexually targeted by their attackers."<ref name="BBC News-2023" /> Testimonies from those at the Shura Base where the victims bodies were brought, such as IDF Captain (Res.) Maayan, who is also a dentist, and Shari Mendes, a volunteer, claimed that there were signs of sexual abuse, including mutilations, broken limbs, and broken pelvises.<ref>{{cite news |last=Hinsliff |first=Gaby |author-link=Gaby Hinsliff |date=December 1, 2023 |title=Whatever your view of the Israel-Hamas war, rape is rape. To trivialise it is to diminish ourselves |url= https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2023/dec/01/israel-hamas-war-rape-israelis-palestinians |access-date=December 14, 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |issn=0261-3077}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |first=Carrie |last=Keller-Lynn |date=November 9, 2023 |title=Amid war and urgent need to ID bodies, evidence of Hamas's October 7 rapes slips away |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/amid-war-and-urgent-need-to-id-bodies-evidence-of-hamass-october-7-rapes-slips-away/ |url-status=live |access-date=November 29, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231111231211/https://www.timesofisrael.com/amid-war-and-urgent-need-to-id-bodies-evidence-of-hamass-october-7-rapes-slips-away/ |archive-date=November 11, 2023}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=December 5, 2023 |title=Hamas accused of using rape as weapon of war in Israel in October 7 attack |publisher=[[American Broadcasting Company|ABC]] |url=https://abc7chicago.com/hamas-rape-accounts-sexual-assaults-israel-october-7-videos/14142200/}}</ref> Some of the released hostages also shared testimonies of sexual violence during their time in Gaza.<ref name="Associated Press-2023"/>

Some witness testimony was subsequently discredited, including the claim shared by among others Shari Mendes of the alleged stabbing of a pregnant woman and her fetus and several alleged rapes.<ref name="intercept-getterman-rebuttal">{{cite web |last1=Grim |first1=Ryan |last2=Boguslaw |first2=Daniel |last3=Scahill |first3=Jeremy |date=February 29, 2024 |title=Between the Hammer and the Anvil: The Story Behind the New York Times October 7 Exposé |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/02/28/new-york-times-anat-schwartz-october-7/ |access-date=April 1, 2024 |website=[[The Intercept]] |publisher=}}</ref><ref>{{bulleted list|
| {{cite news |last1=Rabinowitz |first1=Aaron |date=January 31, 2024 |title=Death and Donations: Did the Israeli Volunteer Group Handling the Dead of October 7 Exploit Its Role? |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-31/ty-article-magazine/.premium/death-and-donations-did-the-volunteer-group-handling-the-october-7-dead-exploit-its-role/0000018d-5a73-d997-adff-df7bdb670000 |access-date=April 1, 2024 |newspaper=Haaretz}}
| {{cite web |last1=Gupta |first1=Arun |date=February 27, 2024 |title=American Media Keep Citing Zaka — Though Its October 7 Atrocity Stories are Discredited in Israel |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/02/27/zaka-october-7-israel-hamas-new-york-times/ |access-date=April 1, 2024 |website=theintercept.com |publisher=The Intercept}}
| {{Cite web |date=May 22, 2024 |title=How 2 debunked accounts of sexual violence on Oct. 7 fueled a global dispute over Israel-Hamas war |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-hamas-war-sexual-violence-zaka-ca7905bf9520b1e646f86d72cdf03244 |access-date=August 11, 2024 |website=AP News |language=en}}
}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last1=Scahill |first1=Jeremy |last2=Grim |first2=Ryan |date=March 4, 2024 |title=Kibbutz Be'eri Rejects Story in New York Times October 7 Exposé: "They Were Not Sexually Abused" |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/03/04/nyt-october-7-sexual-violence-kibbutz-beeri/ |access-date=October 6, 2024 |website=The Intercept |language=en-US}}</ref> ''Haaretz'' reported in April 2024 that "according to a source knowledgeable about the details, there were no signs on any of those bodies [at Shura Base, to which most of the bodies were taken for purposes of identification] attesting to sexual relations having taken place or of mutilation of genitalia." It also alleged that due to the lack of forensic pathologists at most a quarter of the bodies could be fully examined, and for at least one hundred bodies conclusions could not be drawn given their deteriorated state.<ref name="haaretz-evidence">{{Cite news |last=Rozovsky |first=Liza |date=April 18, 2024 |title=15 Witnesses, Three Confessions, a Pattern of Naked Dead Bodies. All the Evidence of Hamas Rape on October 7 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-04-18/ty-article-magazine/witnesses-confessions-naked-dead-bodies-all-the-evidence-of-hamas-rape-on-oct-7/0000018e-f114-d92e-abfe-f77f7e3f0000 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240418162906/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-04-18/ty-article-magazine/.premium/witnesses-confessions-naked-dead-bodies-all-the-evidence-of-hamas-rape-on-oct-7/0000018e-f114-d92e-abfe-f77f7e3f0000 |archive-date=April 18, 2024 |work=Haaretz}}</ref> Israeli forensic pathologists in charge of the process later clarified that all bodies had been examined, and some were disfigured or burned.<ref>{{Cite journal |last1=Mor |first1=Zohar |last2=Kugel |first2=Chen |last3=Mizrahi |first3=Hagar |last4=Kaliner |first4=Ehud |date=November 2024 |title=Mass killing during terror attack at the Israel-Gaza border and the role of the Ministry of Health in identification of human remains and their release |journal=Forensic Science International |volume=363 |pages=1 |article-number=112188 |doi=10.1016/j.forsciint.2024.112188 |issn=1872-6283 |pmid=39128201 |quote=Bodies were delivered to a central mortuary. Each body was coded and undressed for external inspection and documentation of physical elements... Whole-body CT was performed in cases the bodies were disfigured or burned from the second week}}</ref>

A two-month ''[[New York Times]]'' investigation by [[Jeffrey Gettleman]], [[Anat Schwartz]], and Adam Sella, ''[[Screams Without Words]]'', released in late December 2023, reported finding at least seven locations where sexual assaults and mutilations of Israeli women and girls were carried out. It concluded that these were not isolated events but part of a broader pattern of gender-based violence during the October 7 massacres. The probe was said to have been based on video footage, photographs, GPS data from mobile phones, and interviews with more than 150 people.<ref name="NYTrapeinvestigation">{{Cite news |last1=Gettleman |first1=Jeffrey |author1-link=Jeffrey Gettleman |last2=Schwartz |first2=Anat |author2-link=Anat Schwartz |last3=Sella |first3=Adam |last4=Shaar-Yashuv |first4=Avishag |date=December 28, 2023 |title='Screams Without Words': How Hamas Weaponized Sexual Violence on Oct. 7 |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/28/world/middleeast/oct-7-attacks-hamas-israel-sexual-violence.html |access-date=March 5, 2024 |work=[[The New York Times]] |quote=A two-month investigation by The Times uncovered painful new details, establishing that the attacks against women were not isolated events but part of a broader pattern of gender-based violence on Oct. 7. |issn=0362-4331 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240306020559/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/28/world/middleeast/oct-7-attacks-hamas-israel-sexual-violence.html |archive-date=March 6, 2024}}</ref> According to reporting by ''[[The Intercept]]'', the ''New York Times'' investigation has been criticized, both externally and internally by other employees, for apparent discrepancies in witness accounts and lax evidentiary standards.<ref>{{cite web |last1=Grim |first1=Ryan |last2=Boguslaw |first2=Daniel |title=New York Times Puts "Daily" Episode On Ice Amid Internal Firestorm Over Hamas Sexual Violence Article |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/01/28/new-york-times-daily-podcast-camera/ |website=theintercept.com |date=January 29, 2024 |publisher=The Intercept |access-date=February 14, 2024}}</ref> On December 30, ''[[The Daily Telegraph]]'' wrote: "First responders to massacre saw raped and abused bodies, but the rapidity of events—and cultural taboos—may leave the truth uncovered".<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Vasilyeva |first1=Nataliya |last2=Kierszenbaum |first2=Quique |date=December 30, 2023 |title=Why the full extent of Hamas's sex crimes may never be known |url=https://www.telegraph.co.uk/world-news/2023/12/30/truth-about-hamas-sex-crimes-may-never-be-known/ |access-date=January 8, 2024 |work=The Telegraph |issn=0307-1235}}</ref> Al-Jazeera said that "while isolated rapes may have taken place", the "allegations of widespread and systematic rape", allegations it said "were used repeatedly by politicians in Israel and the West to justify the ferocity of the subsequent bombardment of the Gaza Strip", were false.<ref name=ajefalseclaims>{{cite web |last=Unit |first=Al Jazeera Investigative |title=October 7: Forensic analysis shows Hamas abuses, many false Israeli claims |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]] |date=March 21, 2024 |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/3/21/october-7-forensic-analysis-shows-hamas-abuses-many-false-israeli-claims |access-date=March 21, 2024}}</ref> On March 25, 2024, ''The New York Times'' reported that new video had surfaced, contradicting the account of an Israeli military paramedic previously interviewed by the ''Times'' that two teenagers murdered in Be'eri had also been sexually assaulted.<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Rasgon |first1=Adam |last2=Odenheimer |first2=Natan |date=March 25, 2024 |title=Israeli Soldier's Video Undercuts Medic's Account of Sexual Assault |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2024/03/25/world/middleeast/video-sexual-assault-israel-kibbutz-hamas.html |work=[[The New York Times]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250209000606/https://www.nytimes.com/2024/03/25/world/middleeast/video-sexual-assault-israel-kibbutz-hamas.html |archive-date=February 9, 2025}}</ref>

[[Pramila Patten]], the UN's special envoy on sexual violence in conflict, reported in March 2024 that there were "reasonable grounds" to believe sexual assaults including rape and [[gang rape]] took place in multiple locations during the October 7 attacks. Patten also reported receiving "clear and convincing information" that some of the hostages held by Hamas had suffered rape and sexualized torture and that there were "reasonable grounds" to believe such abuses were "ongoing".<ref>{{Cite news |last=Borger |first=Julian |date=March 4, 2024 |title=UN finds 'convincing information' that Hamas raped and tortured Israeli hostages |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/mar/04/un-envoy-reports-on-accounts-of-hamas-raping-and-torturing-israeli-hostages |access-date=March 30, 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]] |issn=0261-3077 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250203065504/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/mar/04/un-envoy-reports-on-accounts-of-hamas-raping-and-torturing-israeli-hostages |archive-date=February 3, 2025}}</ref> The report<ref name=":13">{{cite web |last=United Nations Office of the Special Representative of the Secretary General on Sexual Violence in Conflict |date=March 4, 2024 |title=Mission report – Official visit of the Office of the SRSG-SVC to Israel and the occupied West Bank 29 January – 14 February 2024 |url=https://www.un.org/sexualviolenceinconflict/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/report/mission-report-official-visit-of-the-office-of-the-srsg-svc-to-israel-and-the-occupied-west-bank-29-january-14-february-2024/20240304-Israel-oWB-CRSV-report.pdf |access-date=March 5, 2024 |publisher=[[United Nations]] |archive-date=March 4, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240304224551/https://www.un.org/sexualviolenceinconflict/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/report/mission-report-official-visit-of-the-office-of-the-srsg-svc-to-israel-and-the-occupied-west-bank-29-january-14-february-2024/20240304-Israel-oWB-CRSV-report.pdf |url-status=live}}</ref> stemmed from an unprecedented fact-finding mission to "verify information" and was not a full and legal investigation as Patten's office lacks such a mandate. It was thus unable to establish anything beyond a [[reasonable doubt]].<ref name="Weiniger">{{Cite news |last1=Philp |first1=Catherine |last2=Weiniger |first2=Gabrielle |date=June 7, 2024 |title=Israel says Hamas weaponised rape. Does the evidence add up? |url=https://www.thetimes.com/magazines/the-times-magazine/article/israel-hamas-rape-investigation-evidence-october-7-6kzphszsj |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241008030639/https://www.thetimes.com/magazines/the-times-magazine/article/israel-hamas-rape-investigation-evidence-october-7-6kzphszsj |archive-date=October 8, 2024 |access-date=August 11, 2024 |work=[[The Times]]}}</ref> As American journalist [[Azadeh Moaveni]] reported: "Her office didn't have a mandate to investigate sexual crimes on the ground and had never undertaken such a mission before. I was told by multiple sources at the UN that her trip was a matter of fierce controversy within the organisation."<ref name="Moaveni"/> Patten's report also did not determine that the sexual violence was systematic in nature, did not attribute it to Hamas or other factions, did not find evidence of it being planned, and remained agnostic on its scope. Patten was also unable to find some evidence that Israeli politicians insisted existed, including video and photographic evidence of rape.<ref name="Weiniger" /><ref>{{Cite news |date=April 23, 2024 |title=Israel fumes as UN secretary-general leaves Hamas off sexual violence blacklist |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/israel-fumes-as-un-secretay-general-leaves-hamas-off-sexual-violence-blacklist/ |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20250131032427/https://www.timesofisrael.com/israel-fumes-as-un-secretay-general-leaves-hamas-off-sexual-violence-blacklist/ |archive-date=January 31, 2025}}</ref> The report concludes that "specific attribution of the violations would require a fully-fledged investigation".<ref name=":13"/> Later, Patten, the UN's special representative, requested permission to investigate Hamas's alleged crimes, on condition that her team should also be allowed to access Israeli detention facilities to examine claims of sexual violence by Israeli soldiers, but the request was denied.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Rozovsky |first=Liza |date=January 8, 2025 |title=Israel Blocks UN Probe Into Hamas Sexual Crimes From October 7 to Avoid Inquiry Into Abuse of Palestinians |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-01-08/ty-article/.premium/israel-blocks-un-hamas-sexual-crimes-probe-to-avoid-inquiry-into-abuse-of-palestinians/00000194-44e0-d087-a9bd-7de1d5f20000 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20250126114219/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2025-01-08/ty-article/.premium/israel-blocks-un-hamas-sexual-crimes-probe-to-avoid-inquiry-into-abuse-of-palestinians/00000194-44e0-d087-a9bd-7de1d5f20000 |archive-date=January 26, 2025 |url-status=live |url-access=subscription |work=[[Haaretz]]}}</ref>

The UN's [[Independent International Commission of Inquiry on the Occupied Palestinian Territory]] released an in-depth investigative report on June 12, 2024, which found that both Hamas and Israel had committed sexual violence and torture, along with intentional attacks on civilians.<ref name="OHCHR3"/><ref name="UN Human Rights">{{cite web |date=June 12, 2024 |title=Israeli authorities, Palestinian armed groups are responsible for war crimes, other grave violations of international law, UN Inquiry finds |url=https://www.ohchr.org/en/press-releases/2024/06/israeli-authorities-palestinian-armed-groups-are-responsible-war-crimes |website=United Nations Human Rights}}</ref> The report was created by information compiled from interviews of victims, witnesses, open sourced items, forensic medical reports, and satellite imagery.<ref name="UN Human Rights" /> Israel had previously announced its refusal to cooperate with the inquiry and rejected the allegations.<ref name="CNN coi3">{{cite news |last1=Pokharel |first1=Sugam |last2=Nicholls |first2=Catherine |last3=Yeung |first3=Jessie |last4=Karadsheh |first4=Jomana |date=June 12, 2024 |title=Inquiry says Israel and Hamas have both committed war crimes since October 7 |url=https://www.cnn.com/2024/06/12/middleeast/un-report-israel-hamas-gaza-war-crimes-intl-hnk/index.html |newspaper=[[CNN]]}}</ref> The commission found that Palestinian forces were responsible for incidents "indicative of sexual violence" at the Re'im festival and the Nahal Oz military outpost, as well as several kibbutzim.<ref name="CNN coi3"/><ref>{{cite news |date=June 12, 2024 |title=Report by UN-backed experts cites crimes by Israeli forces, Palestinian militants starting Oct. 7 |url=https://apnews.com/article/united-nations-human-rights-navi-pillay-israel-palestinians-a80c38e1aa2c2090da098f7df20e97fe |newspaper=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref> The report concluded there was a "pattern indicative of sexual violence" by Palestinian forces during the attack, and that Hamas and other militant groups were responsible for gender-based violence "by willful killings, abductions, and physical, mental and sexual abuse".<ref name="CNN coi3"/><ref name="OHCHR3"/> The commission was unable to independently verify testimony of [[Genital modification and mutilation|genital mutilation]], sexual torture and rape, citing a lack of access to witnesses and crime scenes, and Israel's obstruction of its investigations.<ref name="CNN coi3" /> It also found no evidence that Palestinian forces had been ordered to commit sexual violence.<ref name="OHCHR3" /> In addition, the Commission found some specific allegations to be false or contradictory.<ref name="OHCHR3" />

In June 2024, ''[[The Times]]'' published a detailed investigative report concluding that Israel's claims about the scale and the formally sanctioned, systematic nature of sexual assaults did not stand up to scrutiny.<ref name="Weiniger"/>

As of January 2025, the former head of the security cases division in Israel's Southern District prosecutor's office said that no case was being filed due to a lack of evidence and complainants, which she said could be due to victims being dead or unwilling to come forward.<ref>{{Cite web |last= |first= |date=January 6, 2025 |title='We don't have any complainants,' Israeli prosecutor says dept failed to gather evidence on Oct 7 'mass rape' claims |url=https://www.newindianexpress.com/world/2025/Jan/06/we-dont-have-any-complainants-israeli-prosecutor-says-dept-failed-to-gather-evidence-on-oct-7-mass-rape-claims |access-date=July 3, 2025 |website=The New Indian Express |language=en}}</ref>

=== Torture and mutilation ===
{{anchor|Torture}}[[File:Gaza envelope after coordinated surprise offensive on Israel, October 2023 (KBG GPO04).jpg|thumb|Dead bodies after the [[Be'eri massacre]]]]

U.S. Secretary of State [[Antony Blinken]] described photos that Israeli Prime Minister [[Benjamin Netanyahu]] and the Israeli government privately showed him: "a baby, an infant, riddled with bullets. Soldiers beheaded. Young people burned alive. I could go on, but it's simply depravity in the worst imaginable way."<ref>{{cite news |title=Blinken describes images of Hamas attack victims, pledges US support on trip to Israel |url=https://abcnews.go.com/International/blinken-meets-hamas-attack-survivors-pledges-us-support/story?id=103925374 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231114182231/https://abcnews.go.com/International/blinken-meets-hamas-attack-survivors-pledges-us-support/story?id=103925374 |archive-date=November 14, 2023 |access-date=November 15, 2023 |work=[[ABC News (United States)|ABC News]]}}</ref> Israeli forces in [[Kfar Aza]] and [[Be'eri]]<ref name="CNN1nov23">{{cite news |url=https://edition.cnn.com/videos/world/2023/10/31/the-lead-jake-tapper-hamas-atrocities-live.cnn |title=Medics describe atrocities committed by Hamas on Oct 7 |newspaper=[[CNN]] |date=November 1, 2023 |first=Jake |last=Tapper |author-link=Jake Tapper |access-date=November 1, 2023 |archive-date=November 1, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101153242/https://edition.cnn.com/videos/world/2023/10/31/the-lead-jake-tapper-hamas-atrocities-live.cnn |url-status=live}}</ref> reported that they found bodies of victims mutilated. One IDF commander falsely told an [[I24NEWS (Israeli TV channel)|I24NEWS]] reporter that 40 babies had been killed,<ref name="TOI1010">{{Cite news |last=Berman |first=Lazar |title='At least 40 babies |url-status=live}}</ref> Instead, two babies are known to have died as a result of the attack, one from a bullet, and one in a hospital shortly after birth.<ref name=haaretz_atrocities /><ref>{{Cite [[File:Gaza envelope after coordinated surprise offensive on Israel, October 2023 (KBG GPO12).jpg|thumb|Abandoned and damaged cars after the [[Re'im music festival massacre]]]] [[ZAKA]] volunteers acting as first responders spread other false reports of this type.<ref name=haaretz_atrocities /><ref name=haaretz_Rabinowitz>{{Cite news |last=Rabinowitz |first=Aaron |date=January 31, 2024 |title=Death and Donations: Did the Israeli Volunteer Group Handling the Dead of October 7 Exploit Its Role? |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-31/ty-article-magazine/.premium/death-and-donations-did-the-volunteer-group-handling-the-october-7-dead-exploit-its-role/0000018d-5a73-d997-adff-df7bdb670000 |access-date=January 26, 2024 |work=[[Haaretz]] |archive-date=February 9, 2024 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20240209154317/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2024-01-31/ty-article-magazine/.premium/death-and-donations-did-the-volunteer-group-handling-the-october-7-dead-exploit-its-role/0000018d-5a73-d997-adff-df7bdb670000 |url-status=live |quote=Tales of imagination<br />This horrific incident, which the Zaka volunteer alleged occurred in Be'eri, simply didn't happen}}</ref> In one, a ZAKA volunteer said groups of children were found tied up and burned alive.<ref name=haaretz_atrocities /> Other reported atrocities included sexual assaults, rapes, and mutilations; some victims were reportedly bound, and some victims' bodies desecrated.<ref name=haaretz_atrocities /> [[Graeme Wood (journalist)|Graeme Wood]] reported that the video footage retrieved from body cameras the attackers wore showed several victims who "in the beginning of the footage... are alive, [and] by the end they're dead. Sometimes, in fact frequently, after their death their bodies are still being desecrated."<ref name="CBC News">{{Cite news |date=October 25, 2023 |title=Journalist describes footage of Hamas atrocities compiled by the IDF |url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EW0Atcdy38g |publisher=[[CBC News]] |via=[[YouTube]] |access-date=October 26, 2023 |archive-date=October 26, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231026041233/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EW0Atcdy38g&feature=youtu.be |url-status=live}}</ref> Other videos show attackers shooting at children, executing men in civilian clothing, throwing grenades into civilian shelters, and an attempted decapitation.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Carroll |first=Rory |date=October 23, 2023 |title=Israel shows footage of Hamas killings 'to counter denial of atrocities' |work=[[The Guardian]] |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/23/israel-shows-footage-of-hamas-killings-to-counter-denial-of-atrocities |access-date=October 28, 2023 |issn=0261-3077 |archive-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028212742/https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/23/israel-shows-footage-of-hamas-killings-to-counter-denial-of-atrocities |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last1=Estrin |first1=Daniel |last2=Bashir |first2=Abu Bakr |last3=Balaban |first3=Samantha |last4=Harbage |first4=Claire |date=October 27, 2023 |title=New details emerge about the Hamas-led attackers who massacred Israelis |publisher=[[NPR]] |url=https://www.npr.org/2023/10/27/1208836319/israel-hamas-islamic-jihad-militants-videos-details |access-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028190716/https://www.npr.org/2023/10/27/1208836319/israel-hamas-islamic-jihad-militants-videos-details |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=October 18, 2023 |title=Israel/Palestine: Videos of Hamas-Led Attacks Verified |website=[[Human Rights Watch]] |url=https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/10/18/israel/palestine-videos-hamas-led-attacks-verified |access-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028190716/https://www.hrw.org/news/2023/10/18/israel/palestine-videos-hamas-led-attacks-verified |url-status=live}}</ref>

First response personnel recovering the bodies reported being extremely distressed by the evidence of atrocities they encountered, and said they placed the bodies of Hamas militants in body bags marked with an "X" and removed them with a bulldozer.<ref name=":3">{{Cite news |last=Ramsay |first=Stuart |date=October 16, 2023 |title=Israel-Hamas war: Recovered bodies show 'bloodthirsty' gunmen 'took time over torture' – and that Hamas has changed |url=https://news.sky.com/story/israel-gaza-war-recovered-bodies-show-bloodthirsty-gunmen-took-time-over-torture-and-that-hamas-has-changed-12985212 |access-date=October 19, 2023 |work=[[Sky News]] |archive-date=October 15, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231015215425/https://news.sky.com/story/israel-gaza-war-recovered-bodies-show-bloodthirsty-gunmen-took-time-over-torture-and-that-hamas-has-changed-12985212 |url-status=live}}</ref>

Israeli security agencies released videos that the ''Times of Israel'' described as [[Confessions of detained Palestinians in the Israel–Hamas war|alleged confessions]] of Hamas attackers, in which the subjects said they were ordered to kill, behead, cut off limbs and rape.<ref>{{Cite news |author=ToI Staff |title=Kill, behead, rape: Interrogated Hamas members detail atrocities against civilians |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/kill-behead-rape-interrogated-hamas-members-detail-atrocities-against-civilians/ |access-date=October 29, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |archive-date=October 29, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029160226/https://www.timesofisrael.com/kill-behead-rape-interrogated-hamas-members-detail-atrocities-against-civilians/ |url-status=live}}</ref> [[Human Rights Watch]], [[Amnesty International]] and [[Physicians for Human Rights–Israel|Physicians for Human Rights Israel]] stated that these alleged confessions were likely extracted under torture, should not be accepted as credible evidence, and called on the Israeli government to cease their production and publication.<ref>{{Cite news |title=Israel likely tortured Palestinian to record rape confession, say rights groups |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/gaza-israel-war-likely-tortured-palestinian-rape-confession-rights-groups |access-date=August 11, 2024 |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last= |date=November 26, 2023 |title=Gender-Based Violence as a Weapon of War during the October 7 Hamas Attacks {{!}} Position Paper |url=https://www.phr.org.il/en/gender-based-violence-eng/ |access-date=August 11, 2024 |website=Physicians for Human Rights Israel |language=en-US}}</ref>

A former chief rabbi of the Israeli army, part of the team identifying bodies, said there were many instances of rape and torture, and an Israeli reserve warrant officer said that forensic exams had discovered multiple cases of rape, though neither provided forensic evidence to support the claims.<ref>{{Cite news |date=October 15, 2023 |title=Israeli forensic teams describe signs of torture, abuse |publisher=[[Reuters]] |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-forensic-teams-describe-signs-torture-abuse-2023-10-15/ |access-date=October 29, 2023 |archive-date=October 28, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231028215804/https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-forensic-teams-describe-signs-torture-abuse-2023-10-15/ |url-status=live}}</ref> Haaretz reported in April 2024 that no such forensic evidence exists.<ref name=haaretz-evidence /> CNN has interviewed several Israelis who witnessed the aftermath of the attack, who reported visible signs of rape and excessive violence on the bodies of women and girls from several sites.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Tapper |first=Jake |date=November 17, 2023 |title=Video: Witness describes sexual assault of Israeli women by Hamas militants on Oct. 7 |publisher=[[CNN]] |url=https://www.cnn.com/videos/world/2023/11/16/sexual-violence-israeli-women-hamas-attack-tapper-pkg-lead-vpx.cnn |access-date=November 17, 2023}}</ref> ''The Intercept'' called into question the credibility of some of these testimonies, also cited in other reports such as the New York Times' ''[[Screams Without Words]]''.<ref name="intercept-getterman-rebuttal" />

A ''Haaretz'' investigation into the claims of mutilation and torture found that "Members of Hamas and Palestinian Islamic Jihad, as well as other Gazans who entered Israel, committed war crimes and crimes against humanity." Regarding "testimonies about Hamas's atrocities on October 7", ''Haaretz'' found that "Most are supported by extensive evidence, but a few have been proved untrue, providing ammunition to deniers of the historic massacre." ''Haaretz'' found several cases where Israeli search and rescue units, the army, and politicians disseminated inaccurate information. An Israeli army officer claimed that babies had been hung on clotheslines; later investigations showed that exactly one infant was killed, alongside her father, and that the reports of groups of children being slaughtered and mutilated were false. A total of five children under age six were killed, and another 14 between ages 12 and 15 were killed in rocket attacks from Gaza. Most of the children were killed alongside family members.<ref name="haaretz_atrocities" />

''Haaretz'' reported that "Hamas terrorists did desecrate corpses during the massacre, especially the bodies of soldiers. There were also beheadings and cases of dismemberment" but that "there is no evidence that children from several families were murdered together, rendering inaccurate Netanyahu's remark to U.S. President Joe Biden that Hamas terrorists 'took dozens of children, tied them up, burned them and executed them.{{'"}}<ref name="haaretz_atrocities">{{cite news |last=Hasson |first=Nir |title=Hamas Committed Documented Atrocities. But a Few False Stories Feed the Deniers |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=December 4, 2023 |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-04/ty-article-magazine/.premium/hamas-committed-documented-atrocities-but-a-few-false-stories-feed-the-deniers/0000018c-34f3-da74-afce-b5fbe24f0000 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20231220010209/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-12-04/ty-article-magazine/.premium/hamas-committed-documented-atrocities-but-a-few-false-stories-feed-the-deniers/0000018c-34f3-da74-afce-b5fbe24f0000 |archive-date=December 20, 2023 |access-date=December 5, 2023}}</ref> ZAKA volunteers shared stories of atrocities, with one repeatedly describing 20 children having been bound and burned at a kibbutz; the same volunteer said a pregnant woman had her unborn baby cut from her womb and that he had found the woman next to a murdered child aged six or seven. But the list of dead does not correspond to the claims, and no children of that age were killed in the kibbutz; the kibbutz has denied that the story is related to the kibbutz.<ref name="haaretz_atrocities" /> [[Sara Netanyahu]], the Israeli prime minister's wife, sent U.S. first lady [[Jill Biden]] a letter claiming that a heavily pregnant woman was taken hostage to Gaza; the woman was identified as a Thai worker who had been taken hostage and later released. She was not pregnant and had not given birth.<ref name="haaretz_atrocities" />

U.S. Secretary of State [[Antony Blinken]] also repeated some of the evidence given by the same [[ZAKA]] volunteer, describing a scene the volunteer said he found in Be'eri: "a young boy and girl, 6 and 8 years old, and their parents around the breakfast table. The father's eye gouged out in front of his kids. The mother's breast cut off, the girl's foot amputated, the boy's fingers cut off before they were executed."<ref>{{cite web |last1=Shoaib |first1=Alia |title=Hamas militants ate family's meal after they tortured and mutilated parents and 2 young children, Blinken says |url=https://www.businessinsider.com/israel-hamas-gaza-militants-ate-lunch-tortured-mutilated-young-family-2023-10 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231104020341/https://www.businessinsider.com/israel-hamas-gaza-militants-ate-lunch-tortured-mutilated-young-family-2023-10 |archive-date=November 4, 2023 |access-date=November 15, 2023 |website=[[Business Insider]]}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Scahill |first=Jeremy |date=February 7, 2024 |title=Israel's Ruthless Propaganda Campaign to Dehumanize Palestinians |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/02/07/gaza-israel-netanyahu-propaganda-lies-palestinians/ |access-date=March 30, 2024 |website=[[The Intercept]]}}</ref> ''Haaretz'' reported in December 2023 that "no children 6 or 7 or near those ages were killed on Be'eri".<ref name=haaretz_atrocities /> ''The Intercept'' similarly said no one killed in Be'eri matched this account and expressed mystification that U.S. media kept citing ZAKA, even though their testimony was debunked in Israeli media.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Gupta |first=Arun |date=February 27, 2024 |title=American Media Keep Citing Zaka — Though Its October 7 Atrocity Stories Are Discredited in Israel |url=https://theintercept.com/2024/02/27/zaka-october-7-israel-hamas-new-york-times/ |access-date=March 30, 2024 |website=[[The Intercept]]}}</ref>

On October 20, a forensic analysis was presented to the media at Israel's National Center of Forensic Medicine that claimed to show evidence of victims burned alive with bound hands. The analysis suggested that one CT scan of charred remains showed an adult bound to a child at the time of death.<ref>{{Cite news |title=Forensic teams still working to identify bodies 10 days after Hamas massacres {{!}} Israel-Gaza war |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/17/hundreds-of-israeli-bodies-remain-unidentified-10-days-after-hamas-attack |access-date=December 18, 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |date=October 17, 2023}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=November 16, 2023 |title=Inside the Israeli lab 'reassembling and reconnecting' the mangled bodies of the dead |url=https://www.latimes.com/world-nation/story/2023-11-16/la-fg-col1-israel-forensic-pathologist |access-date=December 18, 2023 |work=[[Los Angeles Times]]}}</ref> Many victims were described as having soot in their trachea, indicating that they burned to death.<ref name=":17">{{cite news |last1=Poris |first1=Aaron |date=October 19, 2023 |title=Evidence on Display at Israel's Forensic Pathology Center Confirms Hamas' Atrocities |work=The Media Line |url=https://themedialine.org/top-stories/evidence-on-display-at-israels-forensic-pathology-center-confirms-hamas-atrocities/ |access-date=October 22, 2023}}</ref>

Two or three decapitations of adults or military-age teenagers have been confirmed, one or two IDF soldiers (beheaded after death in combat) and a foreign worker.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Poris |first=Aaron |date=October 24, 2023 |title=Horrific Footage of Hamas Atrocities Revealed by IDF Shakes Global Media |url=https://themedialine.org/top-stories/horrific-footage-of-hamas-atrocities-revealed-by-idf-shakes-global-media/ |access-date=October 27, 2024 |website=The Media Line}}</ref> Adir Tahar, age 19, from the [[Golani Brigade]], was killed in combat by multiple grenades on October 7. After his death, his head was removed and taken to the Gaza Strip where it was found later in the freezer of an ice cream store, inspiring speculation about why it had been taken there. His body was identified by DNA and buried incomplete. The IDF tried to hide from his family that there was only an incomplete body to bury.<ref name="toi - buried incomplete">{{cite news |last=ToI Staff |date=January 18, 2024 |title=Father of fallen soldier: Terrorist decapitated my son, tried to sell head for $10,000 |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/father-of-fallen-soldier-terrorist-decapitated-my-son-tried-to-sell-head-for-10000/ |access-date=June 9, 2024 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref><ref name="JP - 10K">{{cite news |last=Barnea |first=Yuval |date=January 18, 2024 |title=Gazans Tried to Sell Fallen IDF Soldier's Head for $10,000, Says Soldier's Father |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-hamas-war/article-782655 |access-date=June 9, 2024 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]]}}</ref> A second burial ceremony was held after his head was recovered.<ref>{{Cite news |last=ToI Staff |date=February 18, 2024 |title=Sgt. Adir Tahar, 19: Quiet Boy Who Fulfilled Dream of Joining Golani |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/sgt-adir-tahar-19-quiet-boy-who-fulfilled-dreamed-of-joining-golani/ |access-date=October 27, 2024 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref>

=== Unsubstantiated reports of beheaded babies and children ===
{{main|Hamas baby beheading hoax}}

Several Israeli sources said in the aftermath of the attack that there were bodies of multiple beheaded infants in [[Kfar Aza massacre|Kfar Aza]].<ref>{{bulleted list|
| {{cite news |first=Nicole |last=Zedeck |title='It smells of death here': Surveying the scenes of atrocities in Kfar Aza |url=https://www.i24news.tv/en/news/israel-at-war/1696938010-it-smells-of-death-here-surveying-the-scenes-of-atrocities-in-kfar-aza |access-date=October 11, 2023 |work=I24news |date=October 10, 2023}}
| {{Cite news |last=Tuquero |first=Loreben |date=October 13, 2023 |title=Reports of 260 Israeli music fest deaths aren't unsubstantiated |work=[[PolitiFact]] |url=https://www.politifact.com/factchecks/2023/oct/13/instagram-posts/reports-of-260-deaths-at-israeli-music-fest-are-no/ |access-date=October 19, 2023}}
| {{cite news |last1=Williams |first1=Holly |author1-link=Holly Williams (journalist) |last2=Lyall |first2=Erin |date=October 11, 2023 |title=Israel kibbutz the scene of a Hamas "massacre", first responders say: "The depravity of it is haunting" |publisher=[[CBS News]] |url=https://www.cbsnews.com/news/israel-babies-killed-hamas-terror-attack-kibbutz-kfar-aza-first-responders-say/ |access-date=October 11, 2023}}
}}</ref> Later the Israeli government said it could not confirm the veracity of the claim and several investigations found it to be untrue.

In its investigation ''[[Le Monde]]'' concluded that the unverified claim is false, although it became a significant element in the information war, with Israeli authorities intentionally maintaining ambiguous messaging that helped spread the narrative despite lack of confirmation: "Israel has done nothing to fight it and has more often tried to instrumentalize it than deny it, fueling accusations of media manipulation." Some opponents of Israel in turn also instrumentalized the false claim; Pro-Palestinian influencer Sulaiman Ahmed used the claim to deny the reality of Hamas killings, while conspiracist [[Jackson Hinkle]] used it to argue that Israel "has lied about everything." The issue continues to be sensitive, with pro-Palestinian influencers and conspiracists seeing it as "fake news" spread by a "genocidal army of occupation", while on the Israeli side questioning it is likened to [[Holocaust denial]]. "Denied internationally, the rumor remains alive and well within Israel."<ref>{{Cite news |date=April 3, 2024 |title='40 beheaded babies': Deconstructing the rumor at the heart of the information battle between Israel and Hamas |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/les-decodeurs/article/2024/04/03/40-beheaded-babies-the-itinerary-of-a-rumor-at-the-heart-of-the-information-battle-between-israel-and-hamas_6667274_8.html |access-date=November 28, 2024 |work=[[Le Monde]] |language=en}}</ref>

=== Use of hostages as human shields ===
During the October 7 assault, [[Human Rights Watch]] reported two instances where Palestinian militants used Israeli civilians as [[Use of human shields by Hamas|human shields]]. In Be'eri, fighters held civilians in a home and threatened to kill them if Israeli forces attacked. When the Israelis did fire, it led to the deaths of militants and hostages. In Nahal Oz, a fighter used 17-year-old Tomer Arava Eliaz to move between homes and potentially block attacks, and Tomer was later found dead. A purported "hostage detention plan" suggested using hostages as human shields, but its authenticity could not be verified by Human Rights Watch.<ref>{{Cite report |last=Wille |first=Belkis |date=July 17, 2024 |title="I Can't Erase All the Blood from My Mind" |url=https://www.hrw.org/report/2024/07/17/i-cant-erase-all-blood-my-mind/palestinian-armed-groups-october-7-assault-israel |website=[[Human Rights Watch]] |language=en}}</ref>

== Israeli counterattack ==
{{Further|Israeli blockade of the Gaza Strip (2023–present)|Gaza Strip evacuations|Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip|Siege of Gaza City}}

After the initial breach of the Gaza perimeter by Palestinian militants and civilians,<ref name=":18"/><ref name=":19"/> it took hours for the Israeli military to send troops to counterattack.<ref name="MIAGO">{{cite news |title=Many Israelis accuse government's of inept, chaotic response to October 7 massacre |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/many-israelis-accuse-governments-of-inept-chaotic-response-to-october-7-massacre/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231113074458/https://www.timesofisrael.com/many-israelis-accuse-governments-of-inept-chaotic-response-to-october-7-massacre/ |archive-date=November 13, 2023 |access-date=November 13, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref> The first helicopters were launched from the north of Israel, and arrived in Gaza an hour after fighting began.<ref name="HDOIH">{{cite news |script-title=he:הטעיה של חמאס למסוקי צה"ל והכוונת טייסים בוואטסאפ |title=hataya shel chamas lemesuki tza"le vehakavnet taysim bevatsup |trans-title=Hamas deception of IDF helicopters |url=https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/b111niukzt |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231113050601/https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/b111niukzt |archive-date=November 13, 2023 |access-date=November 13, 2023 |publisher=YNET |language=he}}</ref> Israel had difficulty determining which outposts and communities were occupied, and distinguishing between Palestinian militants and the soldiers and civilians on the ground.<ref name="HDOIH" />

The [[Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip]] began at 9:45{{nbsp}}am, and at 10:00{{nbsp}}am Israel claimed responsibility for the attacks.<ref name="at 0945">{{cite news |title=What happened in Israel? A breakdown of how Hamas attack unfolded: 06:45 GMT – Israeli attacks |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/10/7/what-happened-in-israel-a-breakdown-of-how-the-hamas-attack-unfolded |access-date= August 24, 2024 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]] |date=October 9, 2023}}</ref> The IDF declared a state of emergency for areas within {{convert|80|km|mi|sp=us}} of the Gaza border and began targeted actions in Gaza.<ref name="IDF-RT">{{cite web |title=Hamas-Israel War – Real Time Updates |url=https://www.idf.il/en/mini-sites/hamas-israel-war-october-2023/real-time-updates-hamas-israel-war/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231013102344/https://www.idf.il/en/mini-sites/hamas-israel-war-october-2023/real-time-updates-hamas-israel-war/ |archive-date=October 13, 2023 |website=idf.il}}</ref><ref name="bbc-2023-10-08-israeli-tourists-dead-egypt">{{Cite news |date=October 8, 2023 |title=Two Israeli tourists and local guide shot dead in Egypt, Israel says |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67046394 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008120503/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-67046394 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |access-date=October 8, 2023 |publisher=[[BBC News]]}}</ref>

In a televised broadcast, Netanyahu said: "We are at war."<ref name="nyt7oct" /> He also said that the IDF would reinforce its border deployments to deter others from "making the mistake of joining this war".<ref>{{Cite tweet |number=1710622311760413115 |user=netanyahu |date=October 7, 2023 |access-date=October 7, 2023 |language=he |script-title=he:דבריי בפתח ישיבת הקבינט |trans-title=My words at the beginning of the cabinet meeting:}}</ref> In a later address, he threatened to "turn Gaza into a deserted island" and urged its residents to "leave now".<ref name="aj7oct-invasion" /> Israel's [[Security Cabinet of Israel|Security Cabinet]] voted to undertake actions to bring about the "destruction of the military and governmental capabilities of Hamas and Palestinian Islamic Jihad", according to a statement by the [[Prime Minister's Office (Israel)|Prime Minister's Office]].<ref>{{cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Security cabinet says Israel will destroy military, governmental abilities of Hamas, Islamic Jihad |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/security-cabinet-says-israel-will-destroy-military-governmental-abilities-of-hamas-islamic-jihad/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008000150/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/security-cabinet-says-israel-will-destroy-military-governmental-abilities-of-hamas-islamic-jihad/ |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |access-date=October 7, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref> The [[Israel Electric Corporation]], which supplies up to 80% of Gaza's electricity, cut off power to the area.<ref name="bbc1" />

=== Friendly fire and use of the Hannibal Directive ===
{{Main|Hannibal Directive}}

According to a December 2023 [[Ynet]] article, there was also an "immense and complex quantity" of [[Friendly fire|friendly-fire]] incidents during the October 7 attack.<ref name="YnetFF" /><ref name="Cook121215">{{cite news |last=Cook |first=Jonathan |date=December 15, 2023 |title=Why is western media ignoring evidence of Israel's own actions on 7 October? |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/opinion/israel-palestine-war-media-ignoring-evidence-actions-7-october |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215161307/https://www.middleeasteye.net/opinion/israel-palestine-war-media-ignoring-evidence-actions-7-october |archive-date=December 15, 2023 |access-date=December 15, 2023 |url-status=live |work=[[Middle East Eye]]}}</ref> Helicopter crews initially poured down fire at a tremendous rate, attacking about 300 targets in four hours. Later, the crews began to slow their attacks and carefully select targets.<ref name="HDOIH" /> According to ''Haaretz'' journalist Josh Breiner, a police source said that a police investigation found that an IDF helicopter that had fired on Hamas militants "apparently also hit some festival participants" in the Nova music festival massacre.<ref name="haaretz_helo">{{cite news |last=Breiner |first=Josh |date=November 18, 2023 |title=Israeli Security Establishment: Hamas Likely Didn't Have Advance Knowledge of Nova Festival |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-18/ty-article/.premium/israeli-security-establishment-hamas-likely-didnt-have-prior-knowledge-of-nova-festival/0000018b-e2ee-d168-a3ef-f7fe8ca20000 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231118160048/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-18/ty-article/.premium/israeli-security-establishment-hamas-likely-didnt-have-prior-knowledge-of-nova-festival/0000018b-e2ee-d168-a3ef-f7fe8ca20000 |archive-date=November 18, 2023 |access-date=November 19, 2023 |work=[[Haaretz]] |quote=According to a police source, the investigation also indicates that an IDF combat helicopter that arrived to the scene and fired at terrorists there apparently also hit some festival participants.}}</ref> The Israeli police denied the report.<ref>{{cite web |date=November 19, 2023 |title=Israel Police slams 'Haaretz' claim IDF helicopter may have harmed civilians on Oct. 7 |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/israel-police-slams-haaretz-claim-idf-helicopter-may-have-harmed-civilians-on-oct-7/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231119164605/https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/israel-police-slams-haaretz-claim-idf-helicopter-may-have-harmed-civilians-on-oct-7/ |archive-date=November 19, 2023 |access-date=November 19, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref> Subsequent investigation has determined that militants had been instructed not to run so that the air force would think they were Israelis.<ref name="HDOIH" /> This deception worked for some time, but pilots began to realize the problem and ignore their restrictions. By around 9 a.m., amid the chaos, some helicopters started laying down fire without prior authorization.<ref name="HDOIH" /> It is unclear how many hostages were killed by friendly fire.<ref name="Ynet240111" /><ref name="YA240112" /> 

In January 2024, an investigation by Israeli newspaper ''[[Yedioth Ahronoth]]'' concluded that the IDF had in practice applied the [[Hannibal Directive]], ordering all combat units to stop "at all costs" any attempt by Hamas militants to return to Gaza, even if there were hostages with them.<ref name="Ynet240111">{{cite news |last1=Bergman |first1=Ronen |author1-link=Ronen Bergman |last2=Zitun |first2=Yoav |date=January 10, 2024 |script-title=he:ההוראה: למנוע ממחבלים לחזור לעזה 'בכל מחיר', גם אם יש איתם חטופים |title=hahor'a: lemanoa mimchavlim lechzor le'eza tavivkel mechir, gam am yesh itam hatofim |trans-title=The instructions: prevent terrorists from returning to Gaza "at all costs" even if there are hostages with them |url=https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/yokra13754368 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240224193530/https://www.ynet.co.il/news/article/yokra13754368 |archive-date=February 24, 2024 |access-date=January 12, 2024 |url-status=live |work=[[Ynet]] |language=he}}</ref><ref name="YA240112">{{Cite news |last1=Bergman |first1=Ronen |author-link=Ronen Bergman |last2=Zitun |first2=Yoav |date=January 12, 2024 |title=השעות הראשונות של השבת השחורה |trans-title=The first hours of Black Saturday |url=https://w.ynet.co.il/yediot/7-days/time-of-darkness |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240118162157/https://w.ynet.co.il/yediot/7-days/time-of-darkness |archive-date=January 18, 2024 |access-date=January 19, 2024 |work=[[Yedioth Ahronoth]] |language=he}}</ref> According to ''Yedioth Ahronoth'', around 70 burnt-out vehicles on roads leading to Gaza had been fired on by helicopters or tanks, killing all occupants in at least some cases.<ref name="Ynet240111" /><ref name="YA240112" />

A report by a UN Commission published in June 2024 found "strong indications" that the Israeli security forces used the Hannibal Directive in several instances on October 7. <ref name=":63" /> In one example, a tank crew confirmed that they had applied the directive when they shot at a vehicle suspected of carrying kidnapped Israeli soldiers. The report also said that in two instances, Israeli forces "had likely applied the Hannibal Directive," resulting in the killing of up to 14 Israeli civilians.<ref>{{Cite web |title=UN finds at least 14 Israelis likely intentionally killed by own army on 7 October |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/israel-un-killed-own-soldiers-army-7-october |access-date=June 13, 2024 |website=Middle East Eye |language=en}}</ref>

A July 2024 ''Haaretz'' investigation revealed that the IDF ordered the Hannibal Directive to be used, adding: "Haaretz does not know whether or how many civilians and soldiers were hit due to these procedures, but the cumulative data indicates that many of the kidnapped people were at risk, exposed to Israeli gunfire, even if they were not the target."<ref name=":20" /> One of these decisions was made at 7:18 A.M., when an observation post reported someone had been kidnapped at the Erez crossing, close to the IDF's liaison office. "Hannibal at Erez" came the command from divisional headquarters, "dispatch a Zik." The Zik is an unmanned assault drone, and the meaning of this command was clear, ''Haaretz'' reported.<ref name=":20" /> At 10:32 AM, an order was issued to all battalions in the area to fire mortars towards Gaza. Documents obtained by ''[[Haaretz]]'' and the testimonies of soldiers show that use of the Hannibal Directive was "widespread" after an order was issued to the Gaza Division at 11:22 AM that "Not a single vehicle can return to Gaza." 

A source in the Southern Command of the IDF told ''Haaretz'':<blockquote>Everyone knew by then that such vehicles could be carrying kidnapped civilians or soldiers...There was no case in which a vehicle carrying kidnapped people was knowingly attacked, but you couldn't really know if there were any such people in a vehicle. I can't say there was a clear instruction, but everyone knew what it meant to not let any vehicles return to Gaza.<ref name=":20" /></blockquote>At 2:00&nbsp;p.m., all units were instructed not to leave border communities or chase anyone into Gaza, as the border was under heavy, indiscriminate fire. ''Haaretz'' further reported that at 6:40 P.M. military intelligence believed militants were intending to flee back to Gaza in an organized manner from near Kibbutz Be'eri, Kfar Azza and Kissufim. In response the army launched artillery at the border fence area, very close to some of these communities. Shells were also fired at the Erez border crossing shortly thereafter. The IDF says it is not aware of any civilians being hurt in these bombardments.<ref name=":20" />  ''Haaretz'' notes one case in which it is known that civilians were hit, in the house of Pessi Cohen at Kibbutz Be'eri. 14 hostages were in the house as the IDF attacked it, with 13 of them killed.<ref name=":20" />

In a September 2024 report by Australia's [[ABC News (Australia)|ABC News]], former Israeli officer, Air Force Colonel Nof Erez, is quoted as saying: "This was a mass Hannibal. It was tons and tons of openings in the fence, and thousands of people in every type of vehicle, some with hostages and some without." The report also notes Tank officers confirming their interpretation of the Directive, firing on vehicles returning to Gaza, potentially with Israelis on board.
