"My gut feeling told me that they [soldiers from another tank] could be on them," tank captain Bar Zonshein told Israel's Channel 13. <ref name=":75">{{Cite news |date=September 6, 2024 |title=Israel accused of killing its own civilians under the 'Hannibal Directive' to avoid them being taken hostage |url=https://www.abc.net.au/news/2024-09-07/israel-hannibal-directive-kidnap-hamas-gaza-hostages-idf/104224430 |access-date=September 8, 2024 |publisher=[[ABC News (Australia)|ABC News]] |language=en-AU |archive-date=September 9, 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240909021335/https://www.abc.net.au/news/2024-09-07/israel-hannibal-directive-kidnap-hamas-gaza-hostages-idf/104224430 |url-status=live}}</ref>
== Reactions ==
{{see also|Denial of the October 7 attacks}}

=== Allegations of genocide ===
{{Main|Allegations of genocide in the October 7 attacks}}

According to several international law and genocide studies experts, Hamas's assault amounted to [[genocide]].<ref name=":9">{{Cite web |publisher=[[Genocide Watch]] |date=October 19, 2023 |title=Genocide Emergency Alert: Israel and Gaza |url=https://www.genocidewatch.com/single-post/genocide-emergency-alert-israel-and-gaza |access-date=December 7, 2023}}</ref><ref name=":10">{{Cite news |last=Winer |first=Stuart |date=October 15, 2023 |title=Hamas actions are war crimes, could constitute genocide – international law experts |work=[[The Times of Israel]] |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-actions-are-war-crimes-could-constitute-genocide-international-law-experts/}}</ref><ref name=":11">{{Cite news |last=Sokol |first=Sam |date=October 16, 2023 |title=Deadly Hamas Rampage Constitutes 'International Crime of Genocide,' Hundreds of Legal Experts Say |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-16/ty-article/hamas-deadly-rampage-constitutes-crime-of-genocide-hundreds-of-legal-experts-say/0000018b-37d1-d450-a3af-7fddda070000 |access-date=December 7, 2023 |work=[[Haaretz]]}}</ref> Legal and genocide experts have condemned the attack,<ref name="gettleman">{{cite news |last1=Gettleman |first1=Jeffrey |author1-link=Jeffrey Gettleman |last2=Sella |first2=Adam |last3=Schwartz |first3=Anat |author3-link=Anat Schwartz |date=December 4, 2023 |title=What We Know About Sexual Violence During the Oct. 7 Attacks on Israel |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/04/world/middleeast/oct-7-attacks-israel-hamas-sexual-violence.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231204200541/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/04/world/middleeast/oct-7-attacks-israel-hamas-sexual-violence.html |archive-date=December 4, 2023 |access-date=December 4, 2023 |work=[[The New York Times]] |issn=0362-4331}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=November 25, 2023 |title=Israel investigates an elusive, horrific enemy: Rape as a weapon of war |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/11/25/israel-hamas-rape-sexual-violence/ |access-date=December 7, 2023 |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]]}}</ref> saying it represents a serious violation of international law. They argue that Hamas carried out these actions with the intent to destroy the Israeli national group.<ref name=":11" /><ref name=":10" /><ref>{{Cite web |date=October 18, 2023 |title=Legal Experts: Hamas committed War Crimes, Genocide |url=https://www.genocidewatch.com/single-post/legal-experts-hamas-committed-war-crimes-genocide |access-date=December 7, 2023 |website=[[Genocide Watch]]}}</ref> Some commentators point to Hamas's original [[1988 Hamas charter|1988 founding charter]] (not to be confused with the revised [[2017 Hamas charter]]), which [[Calls for the destruction of Israel|advocated for the destruction of Israel]], contained antisemitic language, and, according to certain researchers, implied a call for the genocide of Jews.<ref name=":22">{{Cite news |title=How the term "genocide" is misused in the Israel-Hamas war |newspaper=[[The Economist]] |url=https://www.economist.com/the-economist-explains/2023/11/10/how-the-term-genocide-is-misused-in-the-israel-hamas-war |access-date=December 7, 2023 |issn=0013-0613}}</ref> Some legal experts have suggested that Hamas's targeting of families should be defined as a new crime called "kinocide".<ref>{{cite web |last1= Elkayam-Levy|first1= Cochav|last2= Gilad|first2= Michal|last3= Rudyak|first3= Ilya|last4= Cotler|first4= Irwin|date= March 3, 2025|title= The New Crime of Kinocide
|url= https://lieber.westpoint.edu/new-crime-kinocide/ |publisher= Lieber Institute |access-date=July 14, 2025}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1= Elkayam-Levy and |first1= Cochav |last2= Cotler|first2= Irwin |date= May 20, 2024|title= Kinocide: Hamas targeting of families is a new crime against humanity|url= https://www.timesofisrael.com/kinicide-a-new-crime-against-humanity/|work= [[The Times of Israel]]|access-date=July 14, 2025 |issn=0040-7909}}</ref>

=== Palestinian response ===

==== Hamas ====
[[Khaled Mashal]], the chairman of the Hamas Political Bureau from 1996 to 2017 and later co-chairman, lauded the Hamas attack, calling it legitimate resistance to Israeli occupation. He said, "We know very well the consequences of our operation on Oct. 7", emphasizing that Palestinian lives must be sacrificed in the quest for liberation.<ref name="ArabNews2023Gaza">{{cite web |date=October 20, 2023 |title=Hamas official says group 'well aware' of consequences of attack on Israel, Palestinian liberation comes with 'sacrifices' |url=https://www.arabnews.com/node/2394966/middle-east |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231102073534/https://www.arabnews.com/node/2394966/middle-east |archive-date=November 2, 2023 |access-date=November 2, 2023 |publisher=Arab News}}</ref>

[[Khalil al-Hayya]], a senior member of Hamas and also later a co-chairman of the Hamas Political Bureau, said the action was necessary to "change the entire equation and not just have a clash... We succeeded in putting the Palestinian issue back on the table, and now no one in the region is experiencing calm."<ref name="Hubbard 2023-11-08">{{Cite news |last1=Hubbard |first1=Ben |last2=Abi-Habib |first2=Maria |date=November 8, 2023 |title=Behind Hamas's Bloody Gambit to Create a 'Permanent' State of War |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/08/world/middleeast/hamas-israel-gaza-war.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231111105142/https://www.nytimes.com/2023/11/08/world/middleeast/hamas-israel-gaza-war.html |archive-date=November 11, 2023 |access-date=November 10, 2023 |work=[[The New York Times]] |issn=0362-4331}}</ref>

Taher El-Nounou, a Hamas media adviser, said that he hoped "that the state of war with Israel will become permanent on all the borders, and that the Arab world will stand with [Hamas]".<ref name="Hubbard 2023-11-08" />

[[Ghazi Hamad]], a senior Hamas official, said in an interview: "We must teach Israel a lesson, and we will do this again and again. The Al-Aqsa Flood is just the first time, and there will be a second, a third, a fourth. Because we have the determination...to fight."<ref name="JPostHamad">{{cite web |date=November 1, 2023 |title='We will repeat October 7 again and again' – Hamas official |url=https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/article-771199 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231112091745/https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/article-771199 |archive-date=November 12, 2023 |access-date=November 11, 2023 |publisher=[[The Jerusalem Post]]}}</ref> He emphasized Hamas's willingness to "pay a price", concluding with a call for the elimination of Israel: "We must remove that country because it constitutes a security, military and political catastrophe to the Arab and Islamic nations".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Pacchiani |first1=Gianluca |last2=Bachner |first2=Michael |title=Hamas official says group aims to repeat Oct. 7 onslaught many times to destroy Israel |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-official-says-group-aims-to-repeat-oct-7-onslaught-many-times-to-destroy-israel/#:~:text=A%20senior%20member%20of%20Hamas,future%20until%20Israel%20is%20exterminated |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107182541/https://www.timesofisrael.com/hamas-official-says-group-aims-to-repeat-oct-7-onslaught-many-times-to-destroy-israel/#:~:text=A%20senior%20member%20of%20Hamas,future%20until%20Israel%20is%20exterminated. |archive-date=November 7, 2023 |access-date=November 7, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref>

Hamas denied killing any children in the attack.<ref name="aa3015680">{{cite news |title=Hamas denies it killed children in fight with Israel |url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/hamas-denies-it-killed-children-in-fight-with-israel/3015680 |publisher=[[Anadolu Agency]] |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231104205316/https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/hamas-denies-it-killed-children-in-fight-with-israel/3015680 |archive-date=November 4, 2023 |access-date=November 4, 2023}}</ref> Its official announcement referring to the event rejected the "falsehood of the fabricated allegations" promoted by some Western media outlets.<ref name="aa3015680" /> When asked about the [[Re'im music festival massacre]], where 260 civilians were murdered, Hamas official [[Mousa Abu Marzook]] replied that it was a "coincidence", and that the attackers may have thought these were soldiers "resting".<ref name="economist.com">{{Cite news |date=October 11, 2023 |title=A Hamas leader refuses to admit his group planned to kill civilians |url=https://www.economist.com/middle-east-and-africa/2023/10/11/a-hamas-leader-refuses-to-admit-his-group-planned-to-kill-civilians |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107124816/https://www.economist.com/middle-east-and-africa/2023/10/11/a-hamas-leader-refuses-to-admit-his-group-planned-to-kill-civilians |archive-date=November 7, 2023 |access-date=November 11, 2023 |newspaper=[[The Economist]] |issn=0013-0613}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Hamas says October 7 attack was a 'necessary step', admits to 'some faults' |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/21/hamas-says-october-7-attack-was-a-necessary-step-admits-to-some-faults |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240204194616/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/21/hamas-says-october-7-attack-was-a-necessary-step-admits-to-some-faults |archive-date=February 4, 2024 |access-date=January 22, 2024 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]]}}</ref>

In January 2024, Hamas released a report titled "Our Narrative", which accepted "some faults" but continued to deny having intentionally targeted civilians, blamed Israel for deaths, and justified the attacks as "a necessary step and a normal response to confront all Israeli conspiracies against the Palestinian people".<ref>{{cite news |title=Hamas says October 7 attack on Israel was a 'necessary step' |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/21/hamas-says-october-7-attack-was-a-necessary-step-admits-to-some-faults |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240204194616/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/1/21/hamas-says-october-7-attack-was-a-necessary-step-admits-to-some-faults |archive-date=February 4, 2024 |access-date=January 22, 2024 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera English]]}}</ref>

==== Palestinian Authority ====
On the eve of the Hamas attack at the emergency meeting in Ramallah, Palestinian President [[Mahmoud Abbas]] said that the Palestinian people had the right to defend themselves against the terror of settlers and occupation troops.<ref>{{cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Abbas: Palestinian people have the right to defend themselves |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/israel-palestinians-abbas-idAFS8N3AU0AU |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231104204042/https://www.reuters.com/article/israel-palestinians-abbas-idAFS8N3AU0AU |archive-date=November 4, 2023 |access-date=November 4, 2023 |newspaper=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> According to Palestinian government agency [[WAFA]], Abbas also ordered the government and relevant authorities to immediately send all available resources to alleviate the suffering of Palestinians in Gaza under Israeli aggression.<ref>{{Cite web |url=https://english.wafa.ps/Pages/Details/138006 |title=President Abbas orders immediate dispatch of aid to Gaza amidst Israeli aggression |publisher=[[WAFA]]}}</ref> On October 16, he declared that "Hamas's actions don't represent the Palestinians".<ref>{{Cite news |title=Abbas says Hamas actions 'don't represent Palestinians,' then seems to backtrack |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/abbas-says-hamas-actions-dont-represent-palestinians-then-seems-to-backtrack/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240101210102/https://www.timesofisrael.com/abbas-says-hamas-actions-dont-represent-palestinians-then-seems-to-backtrack/ |archive-date=January 1, 2024 |access-date=January 1, 2024 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |title=President Abbas says Hamas' actions do not represent Palestinians |date=October 16, 2023 |url=https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2023/10/16/President-Abbas-says-Hamas-actions-do-not-represent-Palestinians |work=[[Al Arabiya]] |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240101210102/https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2023/10/16/President-Abbas-says-Hamas-actions-do-not-represent-Palestinians |archive-date=January 1, 2024 |access-date=January 1, 2024}}</ref>

On October 30, [[Hanan Ashrawi]], a [[Palestinian Christian]] official, said the attacks were an act of resistance launched against the IDF.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gilani |first1=Iftikhar |title='This was an act of resistance against the occupation army': Hanan Ashrawi |url=https://frontline.thehindu.com/world-affairs/hanan-ashrawi-spokesperson-for-plo-interview-on-palestine-hamas-attack/article67465345.ece |work=Frontline |date=October 30, 2023}}</ref>

In March 2024, [[Fatah]] – the party that controls the [[Palestinian Authority]] – released a statement accusing Hamas of "having caused the return of the Israeli occupation of Gaza". The Fatah comments came in response to criticism by Hamas and its allies over Abbas' appointment of [[Mohammad Mustafa (politician)|Mohammed Mustafa]] as the new Palestinian Authority prime minister following the resignation of [[Mohammad Shtayyeh|Mohammed Shtayyeh]].<ref>{{Cite news |date=March 15, 2024 |title=Fatah hits back at criticism of new PM by Hamas, other Palestinian groups |url=https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240315-hamas-other-palestinian-factions-decry-naming-of-new-pm |access-date=April 29, 2024 |work=[[France 24]] |language=en}}</ref>

On May 16, 2024, Mahmoud Abbas said that Hamas's unilateral military action on October 7 provided Israel with justification for attacks in the Gaza Strip. He emphasized opposition to harming civilians. In response, Hamas expressed regret for the remarks, asserting that the attack elevated the Palestinian cause and yielded strategic gains.<ref>{{Cite news |date=May 17, 2024 |title=PA's Abbas accuses Hamas of giving Israel 'pretexts' for Gaza war with Oct. 7 attack |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/pas-abbas-accuses-hamas-of-giving-israel-pretexts-for-gaza-war-with-oct-7-attack/#:~:text=%E2%80%9CThe%20military%20action%20that%20Hamas,to%20a%20Channel%2012%20translation. |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref>

==== Palestinian public opinion ====
In November 2023, as a result of Israeli actions in Gaza following the October 7 attacks, Hamas's popularity among Palestinians in Gaza and the West Bank increased significantly.<ref>{{cite news |date=November 21, 2023 |title=Israel's Assault on Gaza Is Making Hamas More Popular and Destroying Hope for a Future Peace |url=https://www.thedailybeast.com/israels-assault-on-gaza-is-making-hamas-more-popular |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231208201526/https://www.thedailybeast.com/israels-assault-on-gaza-is-making-hamas-more-popular |archive-date=December 8, 2023 |access-date=December 10, 2023 |work=[[The Daily Beast]]}}</ref> In a survey conducted on November 14 by the [[Arab World for Research and Development]] (AWRAD), Palestinians showed overwhelming support for the attack. It said, "Palestinians living in the West Bank overwhelmingly answered that they supported the attack to either an extreme or 'somewhat' extent (83.1%)."<ref name=":6">{{Cite news |last=Greyman-Kennard |first=Danielle |date=November 17, 2023 |title=Palestinians in Gaza, West Bank strongly support Hamas, October 7 attack |url=https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/article-773791 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231117235748/https://www.jpost.com/arab-israeli-conflict/article-773791 |archive-date=November 17, 2023 |access-date=November 18, 2023 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]]}}</ref><ref name=":7">{{Cite web |last=Koningsveld |first=Akiva Van |date=November 17, 2023 |title=Three in four Palestinians support Hamas's massacre |url=https://www.jns.org/three-in-four-palestinians-support-hamass-massacre/ |access-date=November 18, 2023 |website=[[Jewish News Syndicate]]}}</ref><ref name=":8">{{Cite web |last1=Azriel |first1=Guy |last2=Grace |first2=Paz |date=November 16, 2023 |title=Survey finds majority in the West Bank support the Oct 7 massacre |url=https://www.i24news.tv/en/news/middle-east/palestinian-territories/1700158968-survey-finds-majority-in-the-west-bank-justify-the-oct-7-massacre |access-date=November 18, 2023 |website=I24news}}</ref> In Gaza, Palestinians exhibited lesser consensus, with only 63.6% "extremely" or "somewhat" supporting the attack. 14.4% answered they neither opposed or supported the attack, and 20.9% opposed the attack to some degree.<ref name=":6" /><ref name=":7" /><ref name=":8" />

By 2024, support for the attacks had significantly dropped. According to a poll published in September by the Palestinian Center for Policy and Survey Research (PSR), 57% of respondents in the Gaza Strip said the decision to launch the offensive was incorrect, while 39% said it was correct. In the West Bank, most still considered the attacks justified despite a decline in support.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Al-Mughrabi |first1=Nidal |last2=Sawafta |first2=Ali |date=October 8, 2024 |title=Hamas faces dissent in Gaza as heavy toll weakens support for war, a year on |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/year-after-oct-7-hamas-faces-dissent-gaza-war-takes-toll-2024-10-08/ |access-date=October 8, 2024 |publisher=[[Reuters]]}}</ref>

=== Israeli response ===
{{Main|Israeli government response to the October 7 attacks}}

[[File:OpenStreetMap image of Northern Gaza Evacuation Line.png|thumb|right|The line in black represents the IDF's boundary at Wadi Gaza for [[evacuation of the northern Gaza Strip]]]]

Israel said that Hamas "made a grave mistake" in launching its attack and pledged that "Israel will win".<ref name="ap1" /> The IDF declared a "state of readiness for war",<ref name="aj7oct" /> adding that reservists were to be deployed not only in Gaza but also in the West Bank and along the borders with Lebanon and Syria.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2023/10/07/Army-says-it-is-fighting-Gaza-militants-who-entered-Israel-by-land-sea-and-air- |title=Army says it is fighting Gaza militants who entered Israel by land, sea and air |date=October 7, 2023 |work=[[Al Arabiya]] |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007112343/https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2023/10/07/Army-says-it-is-fighting-Gaza-militants-who-entered-Israel-by-land-sea-and-air- |url-status=live}}</ref> Residents in areas near Gaza were asked to stay inside, while civilians in southern and central Israel were "required to stay next to shelters".<ref name="bbc1" /> Roads around Gaza were closed by the IDF.<ref name="ap1" /> Tel Aviv's streets were also locked down.<ref name="bbc1" />

After the attack, Israel declared a heightened state of preparedness for conflict.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/07/israel-gaza-rocket-attack-hamas |title=Netanyahu says 'we are at war' after major Hamas attack |date=October 7, 2023 |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |access-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008000139/https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2023/10/07/israel-gaza-rocket-attack-hamas/ |url-status=live}}</ref> The IDF declared a state of readiness for war, and Netanyahu convened an emergency gathering of security authorities. Israeli Police Commissioner [[Kobi Shabtai]] announced that a "state of war" existed, following what he called "a massive attack from the Gaza Strip".<ref>{{Cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Missiles strike southern & central Israel; police declare state of war |url=https://www.jordannews.jo/Section-20/Middle-East/Missiles-strike-southern-central-Israel-police-declare-state-of-war-31321 |access-date=October 7, 2023 |website=JordanNews |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007094646/https://www.jordannews.jo/Section-20/Middle-East/Missiles-strike-southern-central-Israel-police-declare-state-of-war-31321 |url-status=live}}</ref> He also announced the closure of all of southern Israel to "civilian movement" and the [[Yamam]] counterterrorism unit's deployment to the area.<ref name="jordan1">{{Cite news |date=October 7, 2023 |title=Missiles strike southern & central Israel; police declare state of war |url=https://www.jordannews.jo/Section-20/Middle-East/Missiles-strike-southern-central-Israel-police-declare-state-of-war-31321 |website=Jordan News |language= |archive-date=October 7, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231007094646/https://www.jordannews.jo/Section-20/Middle-East/Missiles-strike-southern-central-Israel-police-declare-state-of-war-31321 |url-status=live}}</ref> The IDF's chief spokesperson, Rear Admiral [[Daniel Hagari]], said four divisions were deployed to the area, augmenting 31 preexisting battalions.<ref name="ap1" />

Israeli President [[Isaac Herzog]] said the country was facing "a very difficult moment", and offered strength and encouragement to the IDF, other security forces, rescue services, and residents who were under attack.<ref name="cnn1" />

Ben Gurion Airport and [[Ramon Airport]] remained operational, but multiple airlines canceled flights.<ref>{{cite news |last=Trabelsy |first=Nevo |date=August 10, 2023 |title=Ben Gurion airport stays open as foreign airlines cancel flights |url=https://en.globes.co.il/en/article-ben-gurion-airport-stays-open-as-foreign-airlines-cancel-flights-1001459661 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231008230802/https://en.globes.co.il/en/article-ben-gurion-airport-stays-open-as-foreign-airlines-cancel-flights-1001459661 |archive-date=October 8, 2023 |access-date=October 11, 2023 |work=Globes}}</ref> [[Israel Railways]] suspended service in parts of the country and replaced some routes with temporary bus routes,<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.rail.co.il/?page=special-update-081023 |trans-title=Updates and changes in train traffic until further notice |script-title=he:עדכונים ושינויים בתנועת הרכבות, עד להודעה חדשה |title=adkunim veshinu'im bitno'at harkavot, ad lehodaa hadsha |language=he |work=Israel Railways |access-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-date=October 12, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231012021622/https://rail.co.il/?page=special-update-081023 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |url=https://www.railjournal.com/regions/middle-east/war-with-gaza-cuts-train-services-in-israel/ |title=War with Gaza cuts train services in Israel |work=International Railway Journal |first=Jeremaya |last=Goldberg |date=October 10, 2023 |access-date=October 11, 2023 |url-access=subscription |archive-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011093427/https://www.railjournal.com/regions/middle-east/war-with-gaza-cuts-train-services-in-israel/ |url-status=live}}</ref> and cruise ships removed the ports of [[Ashdod]] and [[Haifa]] from their itineraries.<ref>{{Cite web |url=https://www.cruisecritic.com/news/cruise-lines-change-cancel-itineraries-following-israel-attack/ |title=Cruise Lines Change, Cancel Itineraries Following Israel Attack |work=[[Cruise Critic]] |first=Aaron |last=Saunders |date=October 10, 2023 |access-date=October 11, 2023 |archive-date=October 10, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231010190604/https://www.cruisecritic.com/news/cruise-lines-change-cancel-itineraries-following-israel-attack |url-status=live}}</ref>

==== Capture and interrogation of militants ====
{{main|Confessions of detained Palestinians in the Gaza war}}

Following the attack, more than 600 militants were captured in Israel. Israel has claimed the interrogation of suspects revealed significant insights into the group's strategies, ideologies, and operational methods that played a crucial role in its military response and in shaping the global understanding of the conflict.<ref name="ynetnews2023">{{Cite news |last=Ilnai |first=Itay |title=Detained terrorists: 'Hamas has become akin to animals; they've become ISIS' |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/magazine/article/hjnc0ysx6 |access-date=December 8, 2023 |work=[[Ynetnews]] |date=November 5, 2023 |archive-date=December 22, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231222194840/https://www.ynetnews.com/magazine/article/hjnc0ysx6|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="Ynet20231023">{{Cite news |last=Zitun |first=Yoav |title=An apartment and $10K promised for each Israeli captive, captured terrorist says |url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/hkm3zrvmt |access-date=December 8, 2023 |work=[[Ynetnews]] |date=October 23, 2023 |time=23:06 IST}}</ref><ref name="NBCNews2023">{{Cite news |last=Sanchez |first=Raf |title=Inside Shin Bet's interrogation of 50 Hamas fighters |url=https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/shin-bet-interrogation-hamas-rcna125748 |access-date=December 8, 2023 |publisher=[[NBC News]] |date=November 19, 2023 |archive-date=December 9, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231209101801/https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/shin-bet-interrogation-hamas-rcna125748 |url-status=live}}</ref> Israel's aim was to support its narrative and counter Hamas narratives.<ref name="NBCNews2023" />

However, a number of sources have questioned whether Israel forced Palestinians to make confessions. Some of the militants in the videos appear to be bloodied and in pain.<ref name="guardian">{{cite news |title=UN's António Guterres calls for immediate ceasefire to end 'epic suffering' in Gaza|first= Rory|last=Carroll |date=October 24, 2023|url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/oct/24/un-calls-for-immediate-ceasefire-to-end-epic-suffering-in-gaza |work=[[The Guardian]]}}</ref> On November 14, [[AP News]] analyzed that a confession video Israel released showed the captured militant was speaking "clearly under duress".<ref name="apnews">{{Cite news |last=Federman |first=Josef |date=November 13, 2023 |title=Is Hamas hiding in Gaza's main hospital? Israel's claim is now a focal point in a dayslong stalemate |url=https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-shifa-hospital-ce8fda9821a011a6cb6e4a3df5c90916 |publisher=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref> Palestinians detainees released after October 7 have reported that Israeli authorities ordered them to make statements, beat them severely, and sometimes demanded that they make statements with a gun pointed to their face.<ref>{{cite news |title=The Palestinian teenagers suddenly freed from jail in Hamas hostage deal |url=https://www.ft.com/content/a986d105-4e74-4609-a145-778ac341bf05 |first=Mehul |last=Srivastava |work=[[Financial Times]]}}</ref><ref name=":222">{{Cite web |date=November 8, 2023 |title=Israel/OPT: Horrifying cases of torture and degrading treatment of Palestinian detainees amid spike in arbitrary arrests |url=https://www.amnesty.org/en/latest/news/2023/11/israel-opt-horrifying-cases-of-torture-and-degrading-treatment-of-palestinian-detainees-amid-spike-in-arbitrary-arrests/ |access-date=November 9, 2023 |website=[[Amnesty International]]}}</ref> The UN and reports by human rights organizations such as [[B'Tselem]] and media outlets have confirmed Israeli [[Torture during the Gaza war|systematic use of torture during the Gaza War]], including [[Sexual and gender-based violence against Palestinians during the Israel–Hamas war|rape, gang-rape, sexualized torture and mutilation of detained Palestinian men, women and children]] by Israeli guards, including during interrogations.<ref>
* {{cite news |last1=Borger |first1=Julian |date=March 5, 2024 |title=Palestinians 'beaten and sexually assaulted' at Israeli detention centres, UN report claims |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/mar/05/gazan-detainees-beaten-and-sexually-assaulted-at-israeli-detention-centres-un-report-claims |access-date=March 18, 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]]}}
* {{Cite news |date=July 29, 2024 |title=Palestinians recount deadly abuse in Israeli prisons: 'It is Guantánamo' |url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2024/07/29/palestinian-prisoners-israel-jails-abuse/ |access-date=August 16, 2024 |newspaper=[[The Washington Post]] |language=en}}
* {{cite news |last1=Graham-Harrison |first1=Emma |last2=Taha |first2=Sufian |last3=McKernan |first3=Bethan |last4=Kierszenbaum |first4=Quique |date=August 5, 2024 |title=Torture, abuse and humiliation: Palestinians on Israeli prison 'hell' |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/aug/05/torture-abuse-and-humiliation-palestinians-on-israeli-prison-hell?CMP=Share_AndroidApp_Other |access-date=August 17, 2024 |work=[[The Guardian]]}}
* {{Cite news |title='Raped by female soldiers': Palestinian in leaked Sde Teiman photo speaks out |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/raped-female-soldiers-palestinian-leaked-sde-teiman-photo-speaks-out |access-date=August 16, 2024 |work=[[Middle East Eye]] |language=en}}
* {{cite news |date=August 10, 2024 |title=Palestinian in leaked Sde Teiman photo speaks out |url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2WKeKZ6Csro |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240811152052/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2WKeKZ6Csro |archive-date=August 11, 2024 |access-date=August 11, 2024 |work=[[Middle East Eye]]}}
* {{Cite web |date=August 5, 2024 |title=Welcome to Hell: The Israeli Prison System as a Network of Torture Camps |url=https://www.btselem.org/publications/202408_welcome_to_hell |website=[[B'Tselem]]}}</ref>

[[Human Rights Watch]] and [[Amnesty International]] stated that taped alleged confessions released by the Israeli military were likely extracted under torture, violate international law and basic human rights, and should be considered inadmissible as credible evidence.<ref name="MEE KH">{{cite news |last1=Hearst |first1=Katherine |date=March 29, 2024 |title=War on Gaza: Israel likely tortured Palestinian to record rape confession, say rights groups |url=https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/gaza-israel-war-likely-tortured-palestinian-rape-confession-rights-groups |access-date=July 26, 2024 |work=[[Middle East Eye]]}}</ref> They also called on the Israeli government to cease publishing such taped "confessions".<ref name="MEE KH" /> [[Physicians for Human Rights Israel]] also denounced alleged taped confessions, citing "severe concern that the interrogations included the use of torture."<ref>{{cite news |date=November 26, 2023 |title=Gender-Based Violence as a Weapon of War during the October 7 Hamas Attacks |url=https://www.phr.org.il/en/gender-based-violence-eng/ |access-date=July 26, 2024 |agency=Physicians for Human Rights – Israel}}</ref>

==== Arab Israelis ====
[[File:Isaac Herzog in Rahat, October 2023 (1446).jpeg|thumb|Israeli President [[Isaac Herzog]] in the city of [[Rahat]] with the heads of the [[Negev Bedouin|Bedouin]] community and the families of kidnapped and murdered Bedouins, October 26, 2023]]

[[Arab citizens of Israel|Arab Israeli]] politicians, including the [[United Arab List]] leader [[Mansour Abbas]] and Arab Knesset member [[Ayman Odeh]], condemned the Hamas-led attack on Israel.<ref name="jpost-israeli arabs">{{cite news |last=Teller |first=Neville |date=October 24, 2023 |title=The Arab Israeli community stands in solidarity against Hamas – opinion |url=https://www.jpost.com/opinion/article-769843 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231024064722/https://www.jpost.com/opinion/article-769843 |archive-date=October 24, 2023 |access-date=December 10, 2023 |work=[[The Jerusalem Post]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Arab Israeli Lawmaker Abbas Denounces Hamas Attack, Says the Massacre Does Not 'Represent Our Arab Society' |url=https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-07/ty-article/.premium/arab-list-mk-abbas-denounces-hamas-attack-says-massacre-doesnt-represent-arab-society/0000018b-aa11-d5aa-a19f-affb1b4b0000 |work=[[Haaretz]] |date=November 7, 2023 |access-date=December 10, 2023 |archive-date=December 15, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231215144224/https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-11-07/ty-article/.premium/arab-list-mk-abbas-denounces-hamas-attack-says-massacre-doesnt-represent-arab-society/0000018b-aa11-d5aa-a19f-affb1b4b0000 |url-status=live}}</ref> Israel's Social Equality Minister [[Amichai Chikli]] said, "the Arab population has shown much solidarity and responsibility, and this is especially true for the Bedouin population in the Negev."<ref name="jpost-israeli arabs" />

=== International ===
{{See also|International reactions to the Gaza war}}
[[File:International views on whether 2023 Hamas attack on Israel is a terrorist attack.svg|thumb|Countries that condemned the October 7 attacks as a terrorist attack]]
[[File:3-Popular celebration of Al-Aqsa storm in Iran-%D8%AC%D8%B4%D9%86 %D9%85%D8%B1%D8%AF%D9%85%DB%8C %D8%B7%D9%88%D9%81%D8%A7%D9%86 %D8%A7%D9%84%D8%A7%D9%82%D8%B5%DB%8C %D8%AF%D8%B1 %D8%A7%DB%8C%D8%B1%D8%A7%D9%86.jpg|Celebrations in [[Iran]], October 7, 2023|thumb]]
At least 44 nations denounced Hamas and explicitly condemned its conduct as terrorism, with the denunciations including a joint statement by the United States, the United Kingdom, France, Italy, and Germany. In contrast, Arab and Muslim countries including Qatar, Saudi Arabia, Kuwait, Syria, Iran and Iraq blamed [[Israeli-occupied territories|Israel's policy of occupying the Palestinians]] for the attack. The UAE, Bahrain, and China have amended their initial declarations to expressly denounce the killing and abduction of Israeli civilians.<ref name="WI-Waldo"/><ref name="Guardian-Michaelson"/><ref name="auto2"/> According to a poll conducted by ''[[The Washington Institute for Near East Policy]]'' between November 14 and December 6, 2023, 95% of Saudis did not believe that Hamas had killed civilians in its attack on Israel.<ref>{{cite news |last=Nereim |first=Vivian |date=December 22, 2023 |title=Saudis Overwhelmingly Oppose Ties With Israel, Poll Finds |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2023/12/22/world/middleeast/saudi-arabia-poll-israel-gaza-war-hamas.html |work=[[The New York Times]]}}</ref>

Over 680 legal experts and 128 human rights experts from Israel and around the world have signed an appeal for the immediate release of all hostages kidnapped by Hamas, and for the end of the "vicious and inhumane capture, violence, torture and other cruel, inhuman or degrading treatment of women and girls, children and infants." According to the appeal, "the abductees are defined according to international law as victims of enforced disappearance... [which makes these acts] blatant violations of international human rights law and humanitarian law, amounting to war crimes and crimes against humanity."<ref>{{Cite web |date=October 11, 2023 |title=Law Professors and Human Rights Experts: Holding Hostages in Gaza is a Crime Against Humanity |url=https://www.lawprofsforum.org/post/an-urgent-appeal-from-human-rights-law-professors-oct-9-2023 |access-date=November 8, 2023 |website=The Israeli Law Professors' Forum for Democracy |language=en |archive-date=November 8, 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231108002045/https://www.lawprofsforum.org/post/an-urgent-appeal-from-human-rights-law-professors-oct-9-2023 |url-status=live}}</ref>

The [[United Nations]], particularly the United Nations [[Committee on the Elimination of Discrimination against Women]] (CEDAW), faced criticism for failing to condemn Hamas's actions against women and failing to voice disapproval of reports of [[Sexual and gender-based violence in the October 7 attacks|sexual and gender-based violence against Israeli women and girls]].<ref>{{Cite web |last=Eglash |first=Ruth Marks |date=November 19, 2023 |title=United Nations slammed for silence over Hamas rapes, mutilation and murder of Israeli women, critics say |url=https://news.yahoo.com/united-nations-slammed-silence-over-174157036.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231127024452/https://news.yahoo.com/united-nations-slammed-silence-over-174157036.html |archive-date=November 27, 2023 |access-date=November 29, 2023 |website=Yahoo News}}</ref><ref name="Israeli women testify">{{Cite news |last=Btobl |first=Amelie |date=November 23, 2023 |title=Global women's rights groups silent as Israeli women testify about rapes by Hamas |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/global-womens-rights-groups-silent-as-israeli-women-testify-about-rapes-by-hamas/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231129161152/https://www.timesofisrael.com/global-womens-rights-groups-silent-as-israeli-women-testify-about-rapes-by-hamas/ |archive-date=November 29, 2023 |access-date=November 29, 2023 |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref><ref name="Moaveni">{{Cite news |last=Moaveni |first=Azadeh |date=May 9, 2024 |title=What They Did to Our Women |url=https://www.lrb.co.uk/the-paper/v46/n09/azadeh-moaveni/what-they-did-to-our-women |access-date=August 11, 2024 |work=London Review of Books |language=en |volume=46 |issue=9 |issn=0260-9592}}</ref>

In response Sarah Hendrik, an official from [[UN Women]], one of the UN agencies subject to these criticisms, stated that "within the UN family, these investigations are led by the Office of the High Commission for Human Rights", and that her agency did not have the legal competence to determine culpability.<ref name="Moaveni"/> [[Azadeh Moaveni]] reported that claims of double standards or lack of condemnation by UN Women were incorrect, as: <blockquote>UN Women has not inveighed against conflict-related sexual violence in Yemen, Afghanistan, Somalia, Libya, Colombia or Mali, and its condemnations of rape in the DRC, Central African Republic, Syria and Iraq came years after the events themselves. Where it has responded more swiftly (and then only within months), it has done so in places where the UN had teams on the ground investigating and documenting abuses, or as a result of UN-wide appeals. UN Women has never named a specific group or perpetrator. According to its own protocols, it has been vociferous in responding to October 7 – as many as eight times in the first two months – through statements, social media posts and session remarks.<ref name="Moaveni"/></blockquote> Moaveni also notes that what was demanded of UN Women was to go beyond its mandate and name in an unprecedented way before a proper investigation by the mandated UN bodies had been carried out, and that if it had done so it would have significantly damaged its relationships with grassroots women's groups.<ref name="Moaveni"/>

The [[United States House of Representatives|US House of Representatives]] overwhelmingly passed a bill to amend the [[Immigration to the United States|US immigration code]] and ban people associated with Hamas, PIJ, and other perpetrators of the October 7 attacks from seeking immigration-related relief or protections in the United States.<ref>{{Cite web |last= |date=February 1, 2024 |title=US House passes bill to ban Hamas, other perpetrators of October 7 |url=https://www.i24news.tv/en/news/international/americas/1706747021-us-house-passes-bill-to-ban-hamas-other-oct-7-perpetrators |access-date=February 3, 2024 |website=I24news}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=February 1, 2024 |title=US Reps Bush, Tlaib vote no on 'redundant' bill to ban Oct. 7 terrorists |url=https://www.jpost.com/american-politics/article-784630 |access-date=February 3, 2024 |website=The Jerusalem Post}}</ref> The [[U.S. Department of Justice]] filed charges ''in absentia'' against six Hamas leaders for their involvement in the attacks.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://apnews.com/article/justice-department-hamas-sinwar-87674285aa9b066392953db1310312ca |title=US charges Hamas leader, other militants in connection with Oct. 7 massacre in Israel |newspaper=AP News |publisher=Associated Press |date=September 4, 2024 |first=Eric |last=Tucker}}</ref>

After the attacks, [[USC Shoah Foundation|the Shoah Foundation]] said it had gathered over 100 video testimonies of those who experienced the attacks to add them to the collection of "Holocaust survivor and witness testimony."<ref>{{Cite news |date=December 10, 2023 |title=Shoah Foundation launches project to document 'unspeakable barbarity' of October 7 |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/spielberg-launches-new-project-to-document-unspeakable-barbarity-of-october-7/ |work=[[The Times of Israel]]}}</ref> Shoah Foundation founder [[Steven Spielberg]] said of the attacks, "I never imagined I would see such unspeakable barbarity against Jews in my lifetime" and that the Shoah Foundation project would ensure "that their stories would be recorded and shared in the effort to preserve history and to work toward a world without antisemitism or hate of any kind."<ref>{{Cite news |last=Rosenbloom |first=Alli |date=December 6, 2023 |title=Steven Spielberg comments on 'unspeakable barbarity against Jews' in Oct. 7 attacks |url=https://www.cnn.com/2023/12/05/entertainment/steven-spielberg-october-7-remarks/index.html |access-date=December 15, 2023 |publisher=[[CNN]]}}</ref>

On May 20, 2024, the [[Prosecutor of the International Criminal Court]] requested arrest warrants against Haniyeh, Deif and [[Yahya Sinwar]] for crimes committed during the October 7 attacks, as part of the court's [[International Criminal Court investigation in Palestine|ongoing investigation in Palestine]].<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/c3ggpe3qj6wo |date=May 20, 2024 |title=ICC prosecutor seeks arrest of Israeli and Hamas leaders |newspaper=[[BBC News]] |first=Raffi |last=Berg}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.npr.org/2024/05/20/1252412874/icc-arrest-warrant-israel-hamas-netanyahu-sinwar |title=The International Criminal Court is seeking warrants for Israeli and Hamas leaders |first=Willem |last=Marx |newspaper=[[NPR]] |date=May 20, 2024}}</ref> On November 21, an arrest warrant was issued for Deif accusing him of crimes including murder, sexual violence, torture, hostage taking, [[Extermination (crime)|extermination]] and cruel treatment of the civilian population.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.jpost.com/international/article-830175 |title=ICC issues arrest warrant for assassinated Hamas head Mohammed Deif |newspaper=[[The Jerusalem Post]] |date=November 21, 2024 |first=Eve |last=Young}}</ref>{{efn|Cases against Haniyeh and Sinwar were discontinued, as both had been killed by this date.}} The charges against Deif were dropped in February 2025 after ICC prosecutors confirmed he had been killed in [[13 July 2024 al-Mawasi attack|an airstrike]].<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.newarab.com/news/icc-nixes-arrest-warrant-slain-hamas-leader-mohammed-deif |title=ICC nixes arrest warrant for slain Hamas leader Mohammed Deif |newspaper=The New Arab |date=February 27, 2025}}</ref>

In March 2025, United States Attorney General [[Pam Bondi]] announced the establishment of the Joint Task Force October 7 (JTF 10-7) to seek justice for victims of the October 7 attacks. The task force focuses on prosecuting the direct perpetrators of the attack, pursuing charges against senior Hamas leaders, and targeting individuals and entities providing support or financing to Hamas, [[Axis of Resistance|Iranian-linked proxy groups]], and affiliates. It also addresses acts of antisemitism linked to these groups. JTF 10-7 is led by senior officials from the Justice Department's National Security Division and the [[Federal Bureau of Investigation]], with personnel drawn from multiple DOJ divisions, the FBI, and international partners, including Israel's National Bureau of Counter Terror Finance.<ref>{{Cite web |date=March 17, 2025 |title=Justice Department Announces Launch of Joint Task Force October 7 |url=https://www.justice.gov/opa/pr/justice-department-announces-launch-joint-task-force-october-7 |access-date=August 9, 2025 |website=[[United States Department of Justice]] - Office of Public Affairs}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Rubin |first=April |date=March 17, 2025 |title=Justice Department, FBI launch task force to investigate Oct. 7 attack on Israel|url=https://www.axios.com/2025/03/17/justice-department-fbi-october-7-task-force-bondi-patel |access-date=August 9, 2025 |work=[[Axios (organization)|Axios]]}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Whiteside |first=Steph |date=August 9, 2025 |title=DOJ announces details of Oct. 7 task force |url=https://www.newsnationnow.com/politics/doj-oct-7-task-force/ |access-date=August 9, 2025 |work=[[NewsNation]]}}</ref>

== In culture ==
''[[One Day in October]]'' is a seven-episode [[Anthology series#Television|anthology]] [[Drama (film and television)|drama]] television series based on personal stories from the attacks. It premiered on [[Yes Drama]] in Israel on October 7, 2024.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Brown |first=Hannah |date=October 6, 2024 |title=Anthology series about October 7 to air on anniversary |url=https://www.jpost.com/israel-news/culture/article-822942 |access-date=November 12, 2025 |website=The Jerusalem Post |language=en}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Anderman |first=Nirit |title=A new drama series based on stories from October 7 is sure to impress American viewers |url=https://www.haaretz.com/news/tv/2024-10-09/ty-article/.premium/a-new-drama-series-based-on-stories-from-october-7-is-sure-to-impress-american-viewers/00000192-7113-dfca-adb7-73d303b10000 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20241217203840/https://www.haaretz.com/news/tv/2024-10-09/ty-article/.premium/a-new-drama-series-based-on-stories-from-october-7-is-sure-to-impress-american-viewers/00000192-7113-dfca-adb7-73d303b10000 |date=October 9, 2024 |archive-date=December 17, 2024 |access-date=November 12, 2025 |work=Haaretz.com |language=en |url-status=live }}</ref>

''[[Red Alert (TV series)|Red Alert]]'', another television series based on the attacks, premiered in Israel on October 5, 2025 and internationally via [[Paramount+]] on October 7.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Hibberd |first=James |date=September 25, 2025 |title=Paramount's 'Red Alert' Trailer Depicts Oct. 7 Massacre in Israel for First Time |url=https://www.hollywoodreporter.com/tv/tv-news/red-alert-trailer-oct-7-massacre-israel-1236385547/ |access-date=November 12, 2025 |website=The Hollywood Reporter |language=en-US}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Steinberg |first=Jessica |date=September 24, 2025 |title=Paramount+ to screen Keshet 12's Oct. 7 series 'Red Alert' worldwide |url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/paramount-acquires-keshet-12s-red-alert-series-about-october-7/ |access-date=November 12, 2025 |work=The Times of Israel |language=en-US |issn=0040-7909}}</ref>
